Kigambibwa nti abakungu ba Africa National Congress bano bonna b'amaanyi baaliwo olw'amaanyi ga Masetera.
Okwenyigiramu kw'abantu ab'amaanyi okuva mu gavumenti ya South Africa kuleeseewo obutakkaanya mu nkolagana wakati w'amawanga abiri.
Abanyalwanda abamu ab'omunda era bagamba nti kigootaanyizza okunoonyereza ku kugezaako okukuba Kayumba amasasi.
Ensonda okuva mu Rwanda, yategeezezza Independent nti Karegeya ye yali awa poliisi ya South Africa obubaka ku ani abeera akwatibwa.
Gakwerera naye agamba nti yakwatibwa ku magezi ga Karegyeya.
Okwongerako, Abakungu mu Rwanda bazze malumiriza poliisi ya South Africa obutaba na busobozi.
Bagamba nti amangu ddala nga Kayumba akubiddwa amasasi, abantu abaasooka okutwalibwa okukola sitatimenti ku poliisi be bo be yali nabo mu mmotoka.
Wabula, omukungu okuva e South Africa yasajjula ebintu bwe yayogerera mu yintaaviyu nti gavumenti ya Rwanda ye yali mabega w'okukuba amasasi gano.
Omusango gwa Kayumba gulabise okuteeka enkolagana wakati w'amawanga abiri mu lusuubo olw'obulabe.
Naye waliwo ekisingawo, gavumenti y'e Rwanda yali esabye okukomyawo Kayumba olw'emisango gy'obuyeekera.
Nga 6 Ogwokuna, Spain yawaayo okusaba kwayo okuzza Kayumba olw'emisango gy'okutyoboola eddembe ly'obuntu.
Nga waakayitawo ennaku bbiri Bufalansa nayo yasaba ky'ekimu.
Kayumba yali asobola okugamba nti Rwanda by'emulumiriza nti tebiriimu nsa kubanga ggwanga lyavu nga bye lyogera bisobola okugaanibwa amangu.
Wabula, Bufalansa ne Spain nsi zikirimaanyi ezitwalibwa okuba ne demokolasiya ow'amaanyi n'ebikolwa eby'amaanyi.
N'olw'ekyo, okusaba kwazo kwali kuzito ne South Africa.
Wabula ekyo ekirabibwako, kirinti mu biseera we yakubibwa amasasi, Kayumba yali atandise okukola okusalawo kwe.
Bufalansa ne Spain okusaba okumuzza, kyalaga nti Kayumba ne Kagame baalina beerinako okutya okw'amaanyi.
Okutya kuno kwali kwa maanyi nnyo okusinga ekibaawula.
N'olw'ekyo yatandika okukwatagana ne Kigali.

Buli lwe ntambula mu South Africa, nsisinkana era ne njogerako ne Karegyeya kubanga naye mukwano gwange.

Oluvannyuma n'ankubira ng'agamba nti Kayumba yali akubiddwa esasi n'afa.

Waaliwo abapoliisi bangi nga balina embwa za poliisi.

Mu kukwasisa amateeka, Kalyegira mutuufu okugamba nti eggwanga teriri ku bizimbe, mataala g'oku nguudo oba obuweereza eri abantu.
Ekiseera kikyali okuyita Rwanda olugero lwa Afirika olw'obuwanguzi, ng'era bwe kitali kituufu okuliyita eggwanga erya bulijjo.

Waliwo okukkiriza kwa maanyi nti omukago ogutaba ebibiina gusinga kuddukanyizibwa Federation of Democratic Change.
UPC egamba nti Federation of Democratic Change eddukanya emirimu gy'omukago ogutaba ebibiina awatali kwetabyamu bibiina birala ebirimu.
Ensonda okuva mu Ugandan People's Congress zigamba nti ekibiina kyagala Otunnu avuganye ku bwa mmemba bw'omukago ogutaba ebibiina.

Eyo ye yali entadikwa ya Uganda Patriotic Movement

Abantu bano n'abalala bangi beesanga nga tebasobola kwegatta ku Uganda People's Congress oba ku Democratic Party.

Ekisinze okulemesa eggwanga lya Somalia okutereera ye Amerika
Amerika lwe yasooka okuyingira mu nsonga za Somalia mu 1991 okusingira ddala yalina kigendererwa kya kuyamba bantu baali bakoseddwa.
Naye Amerika bwe yava ku kigendererwa ekyo n'eyingira mu nsonga ez'okuzzaawo emirembe, yatandika okulwanagana ne Mohammed Aideed.
Ekyo kyaviirako Abamerika kkumi na munaana okufiira mu lutalo olwali e Mogadishu, ekyawaliriza Amerika okubiggyamu enta.
Singa Amerika yaleka Aideed okuwamba ensi ya Somalia yonna, Somalia teyandibaddemu butabanguko bungi era yanditebenkedde.
Endowooza n'ebiruubirirwa bya Amerika byeyongera okutumbulwa ebibiina ebirwanirira eddembe ly'obuntu n'abayimbi abaali batamanyi byonna bizingirwamu era abaali babuzaabuziddwa.
Baalowooza nnyo ku ddembe ly'obuntu ne babuusa amaaso obukulu bw'okuba n'eggye erikuuma eddembe mu Somalia.
Nze ku lwange, sikkiriza nti enkola ya demokulasiya awamu n'ebibiina ebirwanirira eddembe ly'obuntu biyamba Afirika.
Demokulase ayamba nsi ezatebenkera edda, so si ezo ezikyalimu obusambatukko.
Somalia kye yeetaaga ye munnamagye ow'amaanyi alina obusobozi obw'okukumaakuma abantu n'okusendasenda amagye amalala.
Mu makkati g'emyaka gya 2000, ekibiina ky'eby'obufuzi ekiyitibwa Islamic Courts Union kyakula era ne kibuna mu bitundu bingi ebya Somalia, ne kireetawo obutembenkevu mu bitundu bingi eby'eggwanga eryo.
Naye oluvannyuma lw'ebyo ebyaliwo nga Ssebutemba 11, Amerika yatandika okwekengera ennyo ekintu kyonna ekyalimu Abayisiraamu, bwe kityo ekibiina ekyo yali ekitwala ng'omulabe.
Yassa ssente mu Esiyopiya esobole okuggyako ekibiina ekyo obuyinza.
Okugwa kw'ekibiina ekyo kwaviirako ekibiina kya Al-Shabaab okutandikibwawo ng'okusingira ddala kyettanira bikolwa bya bwannalukalala mu kifo ky'okuzimba eggwanga eritebenkedde.
Amerika yandibadde ekolera wamu n'ekibiina kya Islamic Courts Union okuleetawo obutebenkevu mu Somalia.
Amerika teyali nneetegefu kusindika magye kukuuma mirembe kubanga bannabyabufuzi mu ggwanga eryo baali tebagyagala.
Bw'etyo yasalawo okukozesa Uganda ne Burundi.

Sikiwa nti ekigendererwa kya Museveni ekikulu kwali kuleetawo mirembe mu Somalia.

Mu 2002, Museveni yagabanako n'abalala ku ebyo bye yayogerera mu lukungaana olwali e Zimbabwe olwali lukwata ku ngeri Uganda ne Rwanda gye zaayambako mu kuggya Mobutu owa Zaire mu buyinza.
Eggwanga lya Somalia okulemererwa okutebenkera n'okutandikibwawo kw'ekibiina kya Al-Shabaab, kivudde ku mawanga ag'ebweru okweyingiza mu by'obufuzi by'eggwanga eryo.
Kizibu okulaba Uganda weefunira mu kuyingira mu nsonga ezo.

Mu butuufu, Obama bwe yali yaakafuuka pulezidenti wa Amerika, yakiraga nti yali tamatira Museveni.
Naye kati olw'okuba omusaayi gwa bannayuganda guyiise okusobola okutuukiriza ebigendererwa bya Amerika mu kitundu kino, kati Obama atwala Museveni ng'omuntu ow'omugaso ennyo mu kutambuza enteekateeka z'alina ezikwata ku kitundu kino.

kindeetera okulowooza nti enkola ya demokulasiya awamu n'ebibiina ebirwanirira eddembe ly'obuntu tebiyamba Afirika.

Ate era n'ekitongole kya poliisi kyali kitegeezeddwa kisobole okulabula abantu ku bulumbaganyi obwali bujja.
Ekitongole kya poliisi kigamba nti waliwo enkuŋŋaana ezimu mwe kyayitira okulabula abantu.
Nga Okitobba 8, 2008, gavumenti we yasisinkanira abantu 24 abaali baava mu ggye lya ADF, kyali kimaze okweyoleka nti waaliwo obuzibu obwali bujja.
Abantu abo abaali baleseeyo obuyeekera basobole okusonyiyibwa baakuumibwa ekitongole ekirwanyisa ebikolwa eby'obutujju nga kyagala babeeko bye bakitegeeza.
Olukuŋŋaana olwo lwali lwa kuwugula aba ADF.
Nga Okitobba 9 omwaka ogwo, olukuŋŋaana olwetabwamu abakulembeze b'amawanga ag'enjawulo lwatuula mu Kampala.
Mu lukuŋŋaana olwo aba ADF baasabibwa okuwaayo ekiwandiiko okuli okwemulugunya kwabwe.
Oluvannyuma baawaayo ekiwandiiko ekyo nga kiteekeddwako omukono gwa Hussein Maiga ne Benz Tushabe.
Okusinziira ku byali mu lukuŋŋaana olwo, abo abaali baava mu ggye lya ADF, aboogerwako nga “balipoota” mu kiwandiiko ekyo baddamu okwogera okwemulugunya kwabwe.
Baagamba nti ssente gavumenti ze yabawa okubayamba okudda mu bulamu obwa bulijjo zaali tezimala era nti baali bawulira ng'abeerabirwa.
Mu kiwandiiko ekyo aboogezi b'eggye lya ADF beemulugunya nti bangi ku bajjaasi baabwe abaaweebwa ekisonyiwo baali bavubuka.
Ekiwandiiko kyagamba nti gavumenti esaanidde okwegendereza engeri gy'ekwatamu abavubuka abo kubanga kyangu abavubuka abo okusendebwasendebwa okuddamu okwegatta ku ggye lya ADF.
Gavumenti esaanidde okuteekawo programu eyamba abavubuka bano Abayisiramu okubaako emirimu gye bakola baleme kufuuka bakireereesi.
Ensonda ez'eby'okwerinda zigamba nti aboogezi ba ADF baali bagezezzaako enfunda n'enfunda okusisinkana pulezidenti Museveni bamubuulire okwemulugunya kwabwe.
Ensonda okuva mu maka g'obwa pulezidenti zigamba nti Noovemba 7 we lwatuukira enteekateeka z'ensisinkano eyo zaali tezinnakakasibwa.
Aba ADF baali baasemba okusisinkana pulezidenti nga Febwali 3, 2004 .
Ku olwo, pulezidenti yalagira nti abakulembeze ba ADF, Maneno Majaliwa ne Sserwanga Bukenya, abaali mu kkomera bateebwe.
Olw'okuba bangi ku bo bakolera wamu n'ebitongole bya Uganda eby'eby'okwerinda era babirimu.
Lipoota eya Agusito 2008 eyafulumizibwa ekitongole ekirwanyisa obutujju.
Mu alipoota eyo ekitongole ekirwanyisa obutujju kyagamba nti aba ADF baali baagala kusaanyaawo abo abaali baabulidde eggye lyabwe.
Alipoota eyo yalimu amannya g'abantu ADF be baali banoonya.
Mu kiseera ekyo, ekitongole ekirwanyisa obutujju kyali kisazeewo okukozesa abakazi nga bambega kisobole okukwata abatujju.

Nga Agusito 8, 2008, baakwatira Joseph Ouma ne Waskile e Busia olw'okuba baali bakolagana n'abantu abaali bateeberezebwa okuba abatujju.
Nga Agusito 10, 2008, Bukomeko Muhammed ne Magelo Shaffik nabo baabalinnya kagere ne bakwatibwa.
Ebikwekweto ebyo byaviirako bangi ku bajaasi ba ADF okwewaayo mu mikono gya gavumenti.
Olw'okuba eggye lya ADF lyazimbibwa ku musingi gwa ddiini.
Abantu abaali baava mu ADF ne bayingizibwa mu kitongole ekirwanyisa obutujju ne mu UPDF baali beetegefu n'okuba nga mu kiseera kye kimu bakolagana ne ADF.
Mu butuufu, bbomu we zaabwatuukira nga Noovemba 7, waaliwo ebyali biyitiŋŋana nti abantu bangi baali beegasse ku ADF.
Lipoota zaali ziraga nti abantu abasinga abaali bayingizibwa mu ggye lya ADF baali batwalibwa mu Democratic Republic of Congo.
Ekitongole ekikessi kyali kigamba nti abantu abasinga ADF yali ebaggya mu buvanjuba bwa Uganda.
Lipoota z'eby'okwerinda empya ziraga nti waaliwo bbomu ezaali zibwatukidde e Kabalagala n'e Lugogo.
Okusinziira ku poliisi, bw'olaba omutwe gw'omuntu nga gukutuse ne gugwa wali emirundi mingi kaba kabonero akalaga nti abatujju babalusizza bbomu.
Eky'okubiri, polisi egamba nti omutwe ogwali gubetentuse e Lugogo gwali gwa Musomaali ate ogwali e Kabalagala gwali gwa Munnayuganda.
Okusinziira ku nsonda z'eby'okwerinda, obwo bwe bukakafu obwasooka okulaga nti aba ADF n'aba Al Shabaab baali bakolera wamu.

Saakamuzooba ziyamba mu butawulira nnyo binnya mipiira mwe girinnya.
Hydrolic w'emmotoka ne sookamuzooba bikolera wamu era emirundi egisinga sookmuzooba bwe zibaako ekizibu kiba kitegeeza hydrolic aliko ekizibu.
Hydrolic wa saakamuzooba zo ayinza okuba nga mazzi ge batadde mu sirinda omuli pisitoni etambulira munda.
Pisitono ekendeeza ku kwegudda kubanga amazzi agali mu sirinda gagikwatirira n'etambula mpolampola.
Sookamuzooba etonnya ebaako obuzibu kubanga ebaamu amazzi matono era ekiseera bwe kigenda kiyitawo gaba tegakyakola bulungi mulimu.
Sakamuzooba zinyumisa okuvuga ekidduka, wadde ng'abantu bangi balooza nti sakamuzooba eziriko obuzibu tekyetaagisa kuzikyusa.
Ekituufu kiri nti okuva ekidduka nga kirina sakamuzooba enfu kya bulabe.
Singa sakamuzooba eba etonnya era ng'eriko obuzibu eba yeetaaga okukyusibwa amangu ddala.
Sakamuzooba ziyamba ekidduka obutegunda nnyo.
Singa sakamuzooba emu oba n'okusingawo ebaako obuzibu kizibuwaza envuga y'emmotoka.
Sakamuzooka ewanirira nnyo emmotoka era ebaako sepulingi waggulu.
Ne ku mipiira egy'emabega kuteekebwako sakamuzooba.
Okusobola okukebera sakamuzooba oba olina okuwanika emmotoka emipiira ne giba nga girengejja mu bbanga.
Kebera buli sakamuzooba olabe obanga waliwo ettonnya.
Zikebere olabe obanga waliwo awakyamye oba awatalazze.
Sakamuzooba zibaako ne nnatti ezisibiddwa mu bbulaasi.
Gikwate waggulu ne wansi ogezeeko okugitambuza ng'ogizza emabega ne mu maaso, oluvannyuma ginyorere awali nnatti.
Bwe wabaawo okutambula kwonna, oba weetaaga okukyusa bbuusi.
Sakamuzooba zikoleko ng'emmotoka ekyawanikiddwa.
Zzuula nnati ya waggulu efaanana n'eya wansi oba zzuula enjola za pisitono.
Bala omuwendo gw'enjola eziri waggulu wa nnatti era ogwo gwe muwendo ogulina okulabika ng'omaze okukyusa sakamuzooba.

Bannamawulire baayanguwa okukuba ebifaananyi bya Otafiire eyali omusunguwavu ng'alina ensonga gy'ategeeza Pulezidenti.
Otafiire ye minisita w'eby'obusuubuzi n'amakolero.
Oluvannyuma lw'eddakiika ssatu ez'akasiriikiriro ak'amaanyi, Pulezidenti Museveni yeenunula mu kattu ke baali bamutaddemu.
Twakakasa ow'ekitiibwa Otafiire nti ensonga ze zikolwako.
 Felistus Magomu, ssentebe w'eby'okulonda mu kibiina kya NRM yagamba nti, "Olukalala lw'abalonzi lujja kutimbibwa mu bifo ebironderwamu.”
Otafiire eyali tasalikako musale yalangirira Mbabazi mu lujjudde nti ssente ze yawa abantu zaali tezimala.
Mbabazi yagambye nti omu ku beesimbyewo yagamba abantu beemulugunye nti baali tebabawadde ssente zimala.
 Otafiire yakyogera lunye nti, "Nze nnagambye abantu okwemulugunya, era nja kuddamu nkyogere.”
Mbabazi, eyasooka ne yeemulugunya, yagamba nti omu ku baavuganya nabo abunyisa ebigambo ebigendereddwa okwonoona erinnya lye ku kuwa abantu ssente.
N'abalala abaali beesimbyewo ku kifo kya Secretary General, Gilbert Bukenya, Elijah Mushemeza, Theodore Ssekikubo, ne Kibibi, baali bamaze okwogera nga bakuba kampeyini yaabwe ey'eddakiika ebbiri.
Mbabazi yamwanukula.
Yanenya Otafiire olw'okumwogerako ebintu ebikyamu nga tasoose kwebuuza kufuna bukakafu.
Abantu abaava mu bitundu by'ewala gamba ng'e Karamoja, Rwenzori, West Nile, Acholi, Lango, ne Kigezi baaweebwa emitwalo asatu zibayambe mu by'ensula.
Mbabazi teyayogera ku bya kaadi ndala na bya kugaana bantu abatuufu kubaawo mu lukungaana olwo nga Otafiire, Bukenya, ne Ssekikubo bwe baali balumiriza.
Museveni teyayita Otafiire kwanukula Mbabazi.
Mbabazi yalabika ng'eyali awangudde abaali bamulumiriza.
Otafiire yasigala agamba abaaliwo nti kino kye kiseera okununula ekibiina kyaffe naye kirabika baamaze dda okusalawo gwe baagala.
N'aba Mbabazi nabo baali bayita mu bantu nga bamukuutira akadingidi.
Naye bo aba Bukenya baali basirise busirisi.
Obuyinza Mbabazi bw'alina mu kibiina kya NRM bungi.
Akulira okulonda ne bwe yajjukiza abantu nti ekiseera ky'okunoonya akalulu kyali kiweddeko, Mbabazi yeeyongerayo eddakiika asatu ng'anoonya akalulu.
Pulezidenti yamala kukyogera nti okunoonya akalulu kuwedde olwo Mbabazi n'alyoka alekera awo.
Ebyali bivudde mu kulonda bwe byalangirirwa, Mbabazi ye yali awangudde n'obululu 5,694.
Abantu abapya baali bazze mu bifo by'abamyuka ba ssentebe mu ggwanga mu bitundu bya Karamoja, mu Bukiikakkono bwa Uganda, mu Massekkati ga Uganda, ne mu Kampala.
Museveni yalondebwa awatali amuvuganya okuba ssentebe wa NRM mu ggwanga era okuba oyo anaakwata bbendera yaabwe mu kalulu kw'oba pulezidenti era ne Moses Kigongo teyavuganyizibwa ku kifo ky'omumyuka wa ssentebe w'ekibiina mu ggwanga.
Rebecca Kadaga yalondebwa okuba omumyuka w'omumyuka wa ssentebe w'ekibiina mu ggwanga era Michael Mukula yalondebwa mu kitundu ky'Ebuvanjuba bw'eggwanga.
Matayo Kyaligonza yawangula Chris Baryomunsi ku kifo ky'omumyuka wa ssentebe mu Bugwanjuba bwa Uganda.
Lwaki Pulezidenti Museveni akyayagala nnyo Mbabazi?
Abaliwo baali bamanyi bulungi engeri Pulezidenti gye yawolerezaamu Mbabazi mu nsonga z'ettaka ly'e Temangalo.
Okuba nti Museveni teyalaga nti Mbabazi yalina ensobi yonna kyalaga bulungi nti abantu abo ababiri enkolagana yaabwe ya ku lusegere nnyo.
Kumpi buli omu eyavaayo okukuba kampeyini yalina okwogera ku linnya lya Museveni okusobola okufuna obuganzi.
Wali okiraba nti buli omu ku baali beesimbyewo yali agezaako okufuna  obuganzi okuva eri Museveni.
Okuva bwe kiri nti ye Muwandiisi omukulu ow'ekibiina, Mbabazi ye yawoma omutwe mu kutegeka okulonda naye kennyini mwe yali omu ku beesimbyewo.
Ku lunaku lw'okulonda, Mbabazi ne be yali avuganya nabo baaweebwa eddakiika bbiri zokka okumatiza abantu nti balina obusobozi.
Ng'oggyeeko okuba nti yali wa nkizo okusinga banne, Mbabazi era mugezi.
Yakola omukago n'abakiise abasinga obungi awamu n'abo abaali beesimbyewo ku bifo by'omu Bukiikakkono, Ebuvanjuba, Karamoja, ne mu massekkati g'eggwanga.
Buli omu ku bantu abo yali yeenoonyeza akalulu ng'ate mu kiseera kye kimu akanoonyeza ne Mbabazi.
Okuvuganya okw'amaanyi yakufuna mu bitundu bya bugwanjuba mwokka.
Mu butuufu Mbabazi yawangula mu bitundu byonna eby'omu bukiikakkono, West Nile, buvanjuba, Karamoja, ne mu massekkati g'eggwanga wadde nga baamulumiriza okugulirira abalonzi.
Abaaliwo baagamba olupapula lwa Independent nti aba Mbabazi baali bawa buli omu eyalonda omutwalo gumu.
Omu ku abo abaali banoonyeza Otafiire akalulu yagamba nti yaweebwa emitwalo ebiri alonde Mbabazi.
Okutwalira awamu ekyo kyalaga enguzi eri mu NRM.
Era eggulo limu enkambi ya Mbabazi yali ekozesezza akakodyo okuyitira ku mikutu gy'empuliziganya era kaamukolera.
Olupapula lwa gavumenti lwagamba nti akakiiko k'ekibiina kya NRM kaali kalagidde Bukenya ne Otafiire okulekera Mbabazi ekifo ekyo.
Ekyo kyaleetawo okubuusabuusa mu bantu abamu abaali baagala okulonda Bukenya ne Otafiire
Ekitundu ekisinga eky'olunaku olwasooka olw'olukungaana, Bukenya yakimala agezaako okumatiza abantu nti ebyayogeddwa emikutu gy'eby'empuliziganya tebyabadde bituufu.
Ebizibu bya Bukenya byali tebinnaggwa.
Olw'okuba baali bakimanyi nti emikutu gy'empuliziganya emirala gyali gisobola okuwandiika ku kulambika kwa Bukenya, olupapula lw'amawulire olwa gavumenti lwabaako kye lukolawo mu bwangu.
Lwaddako ne lugamba nti Bukenya ne Otafiire bajeemedde ekiragiro ky'abakulira ekibiina kyabwe.
Bukenya yali takyalina kakisa kalala kulambika ku nsonga eyo.
Ku ssaawa munaana ez'ekiro ku Ssande, Museveni yayogera eri ab'ekibiina abaali bazze mu lukungaana.
Ng'ayanukula ebyali bigambibwa nti Otafire ne Bukenya baali basambazze ekiragiro kye yagamba  nti, "Ebirowoozo byange nnabitegeezezza Central Executive Committee.” 
Ebifo kkumi na bisatu byokka mu NRM bye byesimbiddwamu.
Obubaka bwaweerezebwa ku masimu nga bulaga nti okunoonyereza mu NRM kulaga nti Mbabazi y'akulembedde banne.
Ku ssaawa emu ey'akawungeezi, obubaka obulala ku masimu bwasindikibwa eri abakiise ne bubategeeza kati Mbabazi ye yali akulembedde.
Kino kiyinza okuba nga kyaleetera abalonzi okwongera okwettanira Mbabazi naye kizibu okumanya bameka abaasendebwasendebwa obubaka obwo obw'oku ssimu.
Ebintu bingi Mbabazi byali bimutambulira bulungi.
Meja Genero Kahinda Otafiire yagenda ku katuuti okukuba kampeyini ku kifo kya Secretary General w'ekibiina.
Amama Mbabazi baamulumiriza nti yali akubye kaadi z'abalonzi endala ng'alina ekigendererwa eky'okubba akalulu.
Obuvuyo obwaliwo mu kulonda bwatabula nnyo ab'ekibiina kya NRM.
Amelia Kyambadde, eyaliko omuwandiisi omukulu owa Museveni yawangula nga tavuganyiziddwa oluvannyuma lw'eyali mu kifo ekyo Ndaula Kaweesi okuva mu lwokaano.
Abakungu ab'oku ntikko mu NRM baali balina bye balumiriza Mbabazi mu lukiiko olwo.
Ng'oggyeeko okumalamu abalonzi baabwe amaanyi, ekyo kyaleetera abakiise okubuusabuusa obanga Bukenya ne Otafiire baali beesigwa eri ekibiina.
Museveni yagamba nti ebyafulumira ku mikutu gy'empuliziganya nti Bukenya ne Otafiire baali bajeemedde ekiragiro kye si bituufu.
Mbabazi yafuna obululu 72 ku buli kikumi, n'addirirwa Bukenya n'obululu 15 ku buli kikumi, Otafiire n'addako n'obululu 13 ku buli kikumi.
Mu butuufu waaliwo okwemulugunya mu bakiise nti ab'omu maka ga Mbabazi baali beefuze eby'okulonda.
Bukenya yabuuza nti, Lwaki obuyinza tetubuwako ku balala?
Ekibuuzo ekyo yali akyolekeza eri ab'omu maka ga Mbabazi.
Muwala wa Mbabazi, Nina Mbabazi, ye yali avunaanyizibwa ku byuma bya tekinologiya w'ekibiina omwali muteekeddwa ebikwata ku buli omu ku bakiise.
Mukyala we, Jacquiline Mbabazi, yalondebwa okuba ssentebe wa NRM ow'ekiwayi ky'abakazi.
Nusura Tiperu eyali amuvuganya yamulumiriza okugulilira abalonzi.
Mukyala wa Mbabazi era ye yali akola ku kuddiza abakiise ssente ze baasaasaanya ku ntambula.
Wooteeri ezaagabula emmere abakiise mu lukungaana olwo ab'oku ludda lwa Mbabazi be baazifuna.
N'abaali baweereza emmere baali bakubira Mbabazi kampeyini.
Obukofiira bwe baayambala bwaliko ebigambo ebikubiriza abakiise okulonda Mbabazi.
Buli kimu Mbabazi kyamuli mu ttaano.
Omu ku bakiise eyava e Mityana yagamba nti, Bbaasi zonna ezaali zitambuza abakiise mu lukiiko olwo zaali zinoonyeza Mbabazi akalulu. Akalulu yali tayinza butakawangula!
Mu lukungaana olwaliwo mu Jjuuni, aba NRM baavumirirwa nnyo ekibiina kyabwe ekyo olw'obutakola bulungi ku byetaago by'abakiise. 
Ekizibu kye kimu kye kyaliwo ne mu lukungaana olw'ebiwayi eby'enjawulo olwaliwo okuva nga 6-9 Ssebutemba.
Abakiise bangi baasimba ennyiriri okumala olunaku lwonna okuweebwa ebyetaagisibwa.
Obutafaananako bibiina birala omwali okuvuganya okw'amaanyi ku kifo ky'anaakwata bbendera mu kulonda kw'obwa pulezidenti ye Museveni teyafuna kuvuganya kwonna mu kibiina kye, ng'ekifo ekyo kiringa ekyamutegekerwa Katonda.
Tewali yamwesimbako.
N'abamu ku abo abaakiraga nti baali baagala okuvuganya naye ku kifo ekyo, baagaanibwa olukiiko lw'ekibiina olukola ku by'okulonda.
Salim Saleh, muganda wa Museveni era wa wansiko mu ranka mu magye.
Ono si ye muntu asobola okuvuganya Museveni.
Mu Maaki w'omwaka guno, ab'ekibiina kya FDC baalonda Doctor Kizza Besigye okubakwatira bbendera yaabwe. 
Baamala emyezi esatu nga bamukubira kampeyini okwetooloola eggwanga.
Okuvuganya ng'okwo tekwaliwo mu NRM e Namboole mu kulonda anaabakwatira bbendera mu kuvuganya ku ntebe y'obwa pulezidenti.
Abo abavumirira NRM bagamba nti ekibiina ekyo kya muntu omu.
Abeekenneenya ensonga bagamba nti ekituufu kiri nti Museveni takkiriza muntu yenna mu kibiina kye kumuvuganya ku bwa pulezidenti bwa kibiina kya NRM.
Bagamba nti okulonda ng'okwo kuyamba Museveni ne NRM okumanya abo abasobola okumuddira mu bigere singa aba akyagadde.
Museveni yasambajja ebigambibwa nti obuvuyo obwaliwo mu kulonda bwe bulaga ki ekibiina kye kye kiri .
Yagamba nti bannakigwanyizi mu kibiina kya NRM baaweebwa obuvunaanyizibwa obw'okuwandiika abantu b'ekibiina mu kitabo kya kyenvu.
Olw'omululu gw'abantu abamu mu kibiina, NRM yawalirizibwa okusalawo okukozesa olukalala lw'abalonzi olw'ekitongole ky'eby'okulonda mu ggwanga.
Yagamba nti obuwumbi buna bwe bwaweebwayo okukozesebwa mu kulonda okw'okusunsulamu mu bifo ebironderwamu kakaaga.
Amangu ddala ng'akirabye nti bamuwangudde, Otafiire yavaawo n'agenda.
N'omumyuka wa pulezidenti, Bukenya, naye teyalinda kulangirira bya nkomeredde.
Abeekenneenya ensonga bagamba nti okulonda okw'okusunsulamu kwalaga nti NRM eri mu mikono gy'abantu abalulunkanira obuyinza.
Eyo ye nsonga lwaki okulonda bwe kwali kugenda mu maaso, okwemulugunya kwonna kwali kwolekezebwa eri Museveni mu kifo ky'okukwolekeza eri akakiiko k'ekibiina akassibwawo okukola ku kwemulugunya kwabwe.
Naye ekyo ye Museveni yakiraba bulala.
Yagamba nti ekyo kyalaga nti ekibiina kya NRM kya maanyi nnyo.
Ab'oku ludda lwa Otafiire baali bakulemberwa Jim Muhwezi ng'akola nga kampeyini maneja ate nga Brig. Henry Tumukunde ng'akola ng'omuwi w'amagezi omukulu mu kulonda.
Baali tebasobola kulumba Mbabazi kubanga pulezidenti yali abalabudde baleme kulumbagana nga bakuba kampeyini.
Otafiire ye yekka eyayoleka obuvumu n'avaayo ne yeekubira kampeyini.
Tumukunde agambibwa okuba omulungi mu kukumaakuma abantu.
Yali tasobola kuddamu kuttusa bizibu bye yalina ne gavumenti ebyali bigenda bikkakkana ng'alumba minisita w'ensonga z'eby'okwerinda era mukwano gwa Museveni ow'oku lusegere.
Abantu nga 350 okuva mu NRM baajulira oluvannyuma lw'okulonda okw'okusunsulamu.
Kino kizibu kya maanyi NRM ky'erina okugonjoola okusobola okwewala okuleka abantu baayo abangi bwe batyo okusigala nga si bamativu.
 Wadde nga waaliwo ensobi ezaakolebwa mu kulonda kwa NRM okw'okusunsulamu, okulonda okwo kweyongedde okunyweza ekibiina.
Okuvuganya okwo kwateekateeka aba NRM ne basobola okulaba engeri esingayo obulungi ey'okukwatamu ebintu.
Yagamba nti akakiiko akakulirwa eyaliko ssaabaminisita Kintu Musoke kaliko Profesa.
Mondo Kagonyera, Moses Ali alondeddwa okukola ku kujulira okwakolebwa. 
Yagamba nti Otafiire ne Bukenya tebaakwatagana na Mbabazi, naye ekyabaviirako obutakwatagana tekyali kituufu.
Opondo agamba nti okuvuganya ku bifo ebitali bimu mu kibiina kulaga abakivumirira nti ddala kirimu okuvuganya.
Yagamba nti okwemulugunya ku Mbabazi bwe kweyongera obungi, yakkiriza ne yeetonda, ekiraga nti yali akkiriza ensobi ze.
Mbabazi ng'akuba kampeyini mu kulonda kw'ekibiina kya NRM e Namboole.
Omumyuka wa Pulezidenti Gilbert Bukenya ng'abuuza abakiise ba NRM era ng'abasaba bamulonde ku bw'omuwandiisi w'ekibiina.
Alex Kamugisha nga munyiivu.
Agamba nti obululu bw'e Rujumbura County bwabbibwa.
Kamugisha asuubirwa okuwanduka mu lwokaano awagire Meja Genero Jim Muhwezi kati avuganya ku kaadi ya NRM mu butongole.
Naye Kamugisha agamba nti tagenda kuva mu lwokaano.
James Tweheyo ye muntu omulala alangiridde nti ayagala kwesimbawo ku bubwe mu munisipaali y'e Mbarara
Tweheyo ne Kamugisha be bamu ku bantu ba NRM abangi abataali bamativu n'okulonda okw'okusunsulamu abaagala okwesimbawo ku lwabwe.
Okulonda okw'okusunsulamu mu NRM tekwatambula bulungi n'akatono ne kiba nti ensonda ezeesigika zaategeeza olupapula lwa Independent nti.
Felicitus Magomu akoze omulimu mulungi okusinziira ku mbeera eriwo, naye ekitongole ky'eby'okulonda kyetaaga omuntu ow'amaanyiko okusinga.
Ku makya nga Ssebutemba 13 bwe yawa okwogera okufundikira mu lukungaana lw'ekibiina.
Daudi Migereko, Chief Whip wa gavumenti yagamba olupapula lwa Independent nti akakiiko ak'enjawulo kagenda kussibwawo okukola ku kujulira.
Engeri akakiiko ka NRM akakola ku by'okulonda gye kanaakwatamu ebimu ku bizibu ebyo ejja kukola kinene.
Nga bali mu lukungaana lwa NRM mu kisaawe e Nambole nga bawagira abantu baabwe abeesimbyewo.
Oluvannyuma Mbabazi yeetonda olw'okutabulwatabulwa okwajjawo.
Baali basuubira abantu omutwalo gumu mu enkumi bbiri naye omutwalo gumu mu enkumi ssatu be bajja
Omuwandiisi w'ekibiina mu nsonga z'okukumaakuma abantu mu ggwanga Maja Genero Mugisha ku bwa pulezidenti w'ekibiina.
Oluvannyuma lw'okufugira emyaka 25, yeeyongera okukiraga nti tannatuusa kuta buyinza.
Yagamba nti bannakigwanyizi mu NRM abaakwasibwa obuvunaanyizibwa obw'okuwandiika bamemba b'ekibiina mu kitabo ekya kyenvu be baavaako obuvuyo mu kulonda okw'okusunsulamu .
Amama Mbabazi awanikira abawagizi ekigalo ng'amaliriza kampeyini ze mu kuvuganya ku kifo ky'omuwandiisi w'ekibiina e Namboole nga Ssebutemba 11.
Ekitongole ekitegeka okulonda kw'ekibiina kirina ebifo ebironderwamu 26,000 era kikozesa obuwumbi obusukka mu 120 okutegeka okulonda.
Hassan Bassajja Balaba avunaanyizibwa ku by'ensimbi, Brigediya Matayo Kyaligonza ne Bernard Mujansi, ssentebe wa disitulikiti y'e Mbale.
Yali tasobola kukubira Otafiire kampeyini kubanga amateeka tegakkiriza bannamagye abakyaweereza okwenyigira mu by'obufuzi.
Oluvannyuma lw'okuwangulwa mu kulonda okw'okusunsulamu okwa NRM okwakamalirizibwa okw'abo abanaakwata bbendera y'ekibiina mu kulonda kwa 2011.
Okusinziira ku ssemateeka w'ekibiina kya NRM.
Bwe bajjukizibwa nti Pulezidenti Yoweri Museveni, Ssentebe w'ekibiina kya NRM era oyo akikwatidde bbendera mu kulonda kw'obwa pulezidenti okwa 2011, yabalabula okwewala obutaba beesigwa eri ekibiina. 
Olukungaana abakungu b'ekibiina mwe baalonderwa wakati mu kuvumagana n'okuyomba, Museveni yaboggola.
Tekimanyiddwa obanga abasinga obungi ku b'ekibiina abaawangulwa baneegatta ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti oba banaasigala mu kibiina kya NRM naye ne bajeemera Museveni ne beesimbawo ku lwabwe.
Okutwalira awamu, abo abaagala okwesimbawo ng'abantu kinnoomu baleeseewo okusoomooza kwa maanyi eri abakulembera NRM.
Daudi Migereko, Chief Whip wa NRM agamba nti, “Abo abeesimbawo ng'abantu kinnoomu baba bazibu okufuga.” 
Migereko yali ayogera ku kusoomooza abeesimbawo kinnoomu kwe bajja okuwa NRM mu kulonda kwa 2011 n'oluvannyuma mu paliyamenti.
Ensonga eyo ekwata ku ba NRM abataali bamativu abaagala okwesimbawo ng'abantu kinoomu yasoosowazibwa mu lukungaana lw'abakulembeze ba NRM olwaliwo mu Jjanwali.
Nga bagenda okufuna olukungaana mu maka g'obwa pulezidenti nga Jjanwali 11;
Omwogezi wa NRM, Muky Karooro Okurut, yanenya abaali baagala okwesimbawo ng'abantu kinnnoomu mu nkola ya Electoral College, eyali ekozesebwa mu kiseera ekyo.
Bwe kityo, abaali mu lukungaana lw'abakulembeze ba NRM mu kugezaako okugonjoola okulumagana okwajjawo oluvannyuma lw'okulonda okw'okusunsulamu baasalawo okukozesa enkola ey'okulonda okw'awamu okwa bammemba b'ekibiina.
Okulonda kwa NRM okw'okusunsulamu okwakakomekkerezebwa kuyinza okuvaako omuwendo ogukyasinzeeyo obunene mu byafaayo by'okulonda ogw'abantu abaagala okwesimbawo kinnoomu.
Karooro Okurut yali yakiraga nti obumu ku buzibu bwe bandifunye bwandibadde bwa ssente ennyingi ezisaasaanyizibwa mu kulonda.
Karooro Okurut yali mutuufu kubanga engeri gye baali balondamu "baali ng'abategeka okulonda kwa mirundi ebiri ”.
Eyo ye nsonga eyaleetera abamu ku ba NRM okutya okuwangulwa mu kulonda okw'okusunsulamu ne basalawo okwesimbawo kinnoomu.
Peter Claver Mutuluza y'omu ku bantu ng'abo.
Ye mubaka wa paliyamenti owa Mawokota South naye yafunamu okutya Amelia Kyambadde, omukazi ow'amaanyi eyaliko omuwandiisi wa pulezidenti bwe yeesowolayo okuvuganya naye ku kifo ekyo.
Amelia alina omukisa munene okuwangula olw'okuba mukwano gwa Pulezidenti wa ku lusegere nnyo era Mutuluza yakiraba nga tasobola kumuwangula.
Agamba nti agenda kwesimbawo ng'omuntu kinnoomu, Lt. Hannington Basakana ne John Banalya abagenda okuvuganya Daudi Migereko e Butembe nabo bali mu mbeera efaananako bw'etyo.
Abalala mwe muli Moses Nagaya agenda okuvuganya ne Nathan Igeme Nabeta mu buvanjuba bwa Jinja, ne Naguib Kezaala...
Okulondebwa kwe mu Wakiso kwaviirako abantu bangi okulumiriza nti okulonda kwalimu okubba.
Okugezesa ekifo ky'omu bugwanjuba bwa Jinja, Moses Kabusu ajja kuvuganya Tim Lwanga ku kifo ky'e Kyamuswa era eyaliko direkita w'ensonga z'eby'obufuzi mu kitongole ekikkessi ne Charles Rwomushana, ajja okuvuganya Jim Muhwezi mu kifo ky'e Rujumbura.
Alex Kamugisha eyawangulwa Jim Muhwezi mu Rujumbura, James Tweheyo eyakwata eky'okusatu mu Munisipaali y'e Mbarara ne Ronah Ninsiima eyawangulwa minisita w'eby'obulimi Hope Mwesige ku kifo ky'omubaka wa paliyamenti omukazi owa Kabale, bajja kuvuganya.
Mu buvanjuba bwa Ndorwa, Charles Musekura awakanyizza obuwanguzi bwa David Bahati mu kulonda okw'okusunsulamu.
Awalala, Zaake Kibedi eyawangulwa Moses Balyeku e Jinja West, Santos Eruaga eyawangulwa Moses Ali mu Adjumani, Alex Onzima eyawangulwa e Maracha, Elizabeth Ociti Alimadi eyawangulwa Betty Bigombe ku kifo ky'omubaka w'abakyala mu Amuru, Kaddunabi Lubega eyawangulwa Faisal Kikulukunyu e Butambala, Beatrice Nyakaisiki Byenkya eyawangulwa Tafasi Kaahwa ku kifo ky'omubaka w'abakyala mu Hoima ne Patrick Isingoma Mwesigwa eyawangulwa Henry Kajura mu Munisipaali y'e Hoima, bagamba nti bajja kwesimbawo ng'abantu kinnoomu.
Naye ebyasinga okwewuunyisa bye bigambo bya Vincent Sempijja eyawangulwa Lule Mawiyae e Kalungu East, ne Samuel Abura Pirir eyawangulwa John Baptist Lokwii e Matheniko.
Ssempijja yagamba nti okwesimbawo ng'omuntu kinnoomu kijja kumuyamba okulwanyisa “ekibba bululu eky'amaanyi ekiri mu NRM,” ate ye Abura Pirir yalangirira nti yali avudde mu NRM.
Ensonda ku kibba bululu mu NRM ne mu kitongole ky'eby'okulonda ziraga nti abantu bonna 1,500 abaajulira bagamba nti obusanduuko bw'okulonda bwakwatibwamu ne kiviirako obululu okusukka ennyo oba okuba obutono ennyo ku obwo obwakubwa mu kulonda ssentebe wa disituliki n'omubaka wa paliyamenti ow'abakyala.
E Kalungu East, Vincent Sempijja yeemulugunya ku butakwatagana wakati w'obululu ku nkalala za NRM n'obw'abalonzi abali ku nkalala z'eggwanga.
Agamba nti wadde ng'enkalala z'abalonzi ez'eggwanga ziraga nti abalonzi abaawandiisibwa bali nga 32,000, abo abali ku nkalala za NRM bagambibwa okuba nga bali 30,853.
Yeebuuza obanga n'ab'oludda oluvuganya gavumenti beenyigira mu kulonda kwa NRM.
Mu Rwemiyaga, obululu 15,466 Patrick Nkalubo bwe yafuna n'obululu 15,423 Ssekikubo bwe yafuna bulaga nti abalonzi ba NRM mu kitundu ekyo baali 31,480.
Obululu 39,884 minisita ow'ensonga z'ebweru Sam Kuteesa bwe yafuna bw'obugatta ku bululu 14,693 banne ababiri, Isha Ntumwa ne Vincent Kimbugwe, abaali bamuvuganya bwe baafuna,  bulaga nti e Mawogola abantu 44,577 be baalonda.
Ensonda mu NRM ziraga nti omuwendo gw'ab'ekibiina ekyo abaagala okwesimbawo kinnoomu gweyongedde nnyo ekireeseewo obweraliikirivu nti bayinza okusalawo okukola ekibiina ky'eby'obufuzi ekirala oba okwegatta ku bawakanya gavumenti ne beefuga paliyamenti.
Ekibiina kya NRM amaanyi gaakyo agasinga obungi gali mu kwefuga ekitongole ekiteesi ky'amateeka era kissa ssente nnyingi mu kukakasa nti kiba n'omuwendo gw'abakiise abasinga obungi mu paliyamenti.
Mu nkola empya ey'ebibiina by'obufuzi, ekibiina kya NRM ekisinga okuba n'omuwendo gw'abakiise mu paliyamenti kyasalawo ebintu ebisinga obungi okubisalirawo mu lukiiko lw'ababaka ba paliyamenti aba NRM oluvannyuma ne babyanjulira paliyamenti okubisemba.
Nye tekibadde na nkola ya kukwatamu kwemulugunya, naddala okwo okuva mu abo abeesimbawo kinnoomu.
Waliwo ebibonerezo ebitali bimu ebibagiddwa okukangavvula bamemba ba NRM ab'omu paliyamenti, omuli okunenyezebwa mu bigambo oba mu buwandiike oyo avunaanyizibwa ku mpisa , okugobwa mu luliiko, okuggibwako obuyinza, oba ensonga okugikwasa ebitongole by'ekibiina ebikwasisa empisa.
Mu paliyamenti ey'omunaana mulimu bamemba ba paliyamenti 38 abeesimbawo kinnoomu, nga baabulako omu okuweza omuwendo gw'ab'ekibiina kya FDC, ekibiina ekivuganya gavumenti ekisingayo obunene.
Ku abo abeesimbawo kinoomu kwaliko aba NRM 32 abataali bamativu na kulonda kwa mu kibiina kyabwe.
Abamu baatuuka ku kukkaanya n'ekibiina kya NRM, naye Chief Whip Migereko agamba nti ekyo tekibalemesa kuwakanya nsonga za kibiina mu paliyamenti era ssemateeka w'ekibiina aba takyabakolako.
Etteeka erikwata ku beesimbawo kinnoomu, etteeka ery'okuna mu ssemateeka w'ekibiina, erikwata ku nneeyisa etekkirizibwa lyogera ku kugobebwa okuva mu kibiina memba yenna oba omukulembeze wa NRM avuganya omuntu ekibiina gwe kisimbyewo mu butongole, oba awa ssente oyo amuvuganya, naye n'okutuusa leero kikyali kizibu okussa etteeka eryo mu nkola.
Mu kulonda okwa  2008 okujjuza ekifo kya Bugembe Town Council, Migereko ne Deputy Resident District Commissioner wa Tororo, Richard Gulume baawagira Sula Sentongo eyali yeesimbyewo yekka eyavuganya era n'awangula Frank Kayemba ekibiina gwe kyali kisimbyewo mu butongole.
Migereko ne Gulume tebaabonerezebwa.
Wadde nga tekirambikibwa bulungi, akawayiro 83 mu ssemateeka wa Uganda akakwata ku bifo by'obwa memba wa paliyamenti, kagamba nti omuntu alekera awo okuba ku ssiga eriteesi ly'amateeka singa ayabulira ekibiina kye baamulonderamu okujja mu paliyamenti ne yeegatta ku kibiina ekirala oba n'asigala mu paliyamenti ng'omuntu kinnoomu, oba singa yajja yekka naye oluvannyuma ne yeegatta ku kibiina ky'obufuzi ekimu.
Olw'okuba etteeka eryo libakolera, abo abaawangulwa balina ebbeetu okuvuganya mu kalulu ka 2011 ng'abantu kinnoomu era ne bafuuka nsonga mu paliyamenti.

Kusoomooza ki kw'osanze mu Private Sector Foundation Uganda?
Okusoomooza okusinga obunene okuliwo kwe kukwanaganya eby'enfuna mu mukago gw'amawanga agali mu buvanjuba bwa Afirika.
Sipiidi ebintu kwe bitambulira tesobozesa bantu bakola bizineesi za bwannannyini mu Uganda kuvuganya bulungi mu butale.
Bye twetaaga okukolako nga Uganda n'abantu abalina bizineesi ez'obwannannyini bingi okusinga ku bya bannaffe mu mawanga amalala be tulina okukolagana nabo mu bizineesi.
Obukwakulizo Uganda bw'essaawo bunyiga yo yennyini kubanga ekyo kigiremesa okutunda ebintu byayo mu butale mu mawanga agali ku muliraano n'ago agali ewala.
Kino kijja kuyamba mu kusitula ekifo Uganda ky'erina mu kitundu olw'okuvuganya okunaabaawo.
Ekitongole kya Private Sector Foundation Uganda era kikolera wamu n'ebibiina ebitali bimu okubisobozesa okuba n'obusobozi bwe byetaaga okuddukanya bizineesi.
Ekibiina kya Private Sector Foundation Uganda kinaaba na kifo ki mu katale ak'awamu ak'amawanga agali mu buvanjuba bwa Afirika?
Omulimu omukulu ogw'ekitongole kya Private Sector Foundation Uganda kwe kubangula abaddukanya bizineesi n'abantu okutwalira awamu n'okubunyisa obubaka obukwata ku bwegassi.
Olowooza akatale ak'awamu kanaakwata katya ku Uganda?
Akatale ak'awamu ak'amawanga agali mu buvanjuba bwa Afirika kagendereddwa okuwa abasuubuzi eddembe okwetaaya
Naye Uganda tenneetegekera bulungi katale ako ak'awamu ak'amawanga agali mu buvanjuba bwa Afirika.
Ekyo kiyinza okulemesa kampuni za Uganda okuvuganya obulungi mu katale ako n'obutakola bulungi magoba.
Ekitongole ekikwanaganya bizineesi ez'obwannannyini, Private Sector Foundation Uganda, kinaaba na buvunaanyizibwa ki mu katale ak'awamu ak'amawanga agali mu buvanjuba bwa Afirika?
Ebiseera eby'omu maaso eby'ekitongole kya Private Sector Foundation Uganda ne bizineesi ez'obwannannyini eziri mu Uganda bitangaavu nnaddala bw'olowooza ku mikisa egiba gigguddwawo.

Fortirwari Karamira  yali Mutuusi era nga wa kibiina kya Republic Democratic Movement ekya Faustin Twagiramungu mu Rwanda.
Mu 1992, yagamba nti yali takyali Mutuusi, n'agamba nti ye Muhutu, era ne yeegatta ku kibinja ky'Abahutu bannalukalala.
Yeekutula ku kibiina kya Republic Democratic Movement asobole okukulembera ekiwayi kyako ekya bannalukalala.
Oluvannyuma, Karamira yateekateeka ekittabantu omwafiira omuwendo gw'Abatuusi ogukyasinzeeyo obunene.
Kajuga, ye yali omukulembeze w'ekibiina kya Interahamwe ekyawoma omutwe mu kittabantu, era naye yagamba nti takyali Mutuusi nti kati yali Muhutu.

Gavumenti ya Habyarimana yalina okukaka abantu okufuna ndagamuntu.

Mukyala we Mutuusi.
Mu kulwanyisa Abatuusi abo, Kayibanda teyakikola lwa kuba nti yabalinako obukyayi naye yakikola lwa nsonga za bya bufuzi .
Enkolagana wakati w'Abahutu n'Abatuusi era yeeyongera okuba enzibu okutegeera bw'olondoola engeri abantu mu Rwanda gye bazze bakolaganamu.
Michel Makuza ye taata wa ssaabaminisita wa Rwanda aliko, Bernard Makuza.
Y'omu ku baali abawi b'amagezi mu kulwana okwaliwo mu 1959 era yali nfanfe wa Kayibanda.
Mukazi we yali Mutuusi era abamu bagamba nti mukazi we alina oluganda olwewala ku Pulezidenti Paul Kagame.
Mukyala w'omugenzi Seth Sendashonga naye kigambibwa nti Mutuusi era nti alina oluganda olwewala ku Kagame.
Kizibu okusanga Omuhutu oba Omutuusi yennyini, atalina banganda mu limu ku mawanga ago.
Ebyo ebigambibwa nti Abahutu n'Abatuusi beerinako obukyayi bungi tebiriiko mutwe na magulu.
Lowooza ku byaliwo mu Rwanda mu 1994.
Gavumenti ya Habyarimana yafuba nnyo okukunga Abahutu obutakkirizanga Batuusi kufuga ggwanga.
Naye Abatuusi be yali agamba nabo baali ba musaayi mutabike.
Habyarimana yali asibuka mu bitundu by'ebukiikakkono ebyavaamu abasirikale b'eggye ly'eggwanga mu kiseera ky'abafuzi b'amatwale.
Yali yawangula Kayibanda eyasibuka mu bukiikaddyo omwali muva abantu abayivu mu kiseera ky'abafuzi b'amatwale.
Eby'obufuzi ebyesigamiziddwa ku mawanga bipya nnyo mu Afirika nga bw'olaba ipad, era bitandikibwawo abantu abeetwala okuba aba waggulu.
Ddala Abahutu n'Abatuusi mu Rwanda balina obukyayi bwonna obuvudde edda?
Habyarimana obufuzi bwe yabutandika na kufuba kusaanyaawo abantu abayivu ab'omu bukiikaddyo, nga muno mwe mwali n'okulumya Kayibanda enjala okutuusa lwe yafa.
Ekyo kyaleetawo enjawukana wakati w'Abahutu ab'omu bukiikakkono n'ab'omu bukiikaddyo.
Obufuzi bwa Habyarimana bwe bweyongera okukakata, enjawukana mu Bahutu zeeyongera ku luno ne zizingiramu n'ebika.
Habyarimana yali ava mu kika kya Mushiru era ne gavumenti ye bw'etyo bwe yali etunuulirwa.
Abantu b'oku kyalo Habyarimana gy'ava n'ab'okukyalo kya Gisenyi gye yajja omukyala, beeyongera okuweebwa ebifo mu gavumenti.
Ekyo kyaviirako enjawukana okulanda ne zizingiramu ebika ne disitulikiti abantu gye basibuka.
Abahutu mu disitulikiti endala baatandika okunenya Habyarimana olw'okusosola mu bantu.
Ekibiina kya MDR kyatandikibwawo nga kino emabega kye kyali ekibiina kya Kayibanda ekyali kikulemberwa Faustin Twagiramungu.
Mu butuufu, mukyala wa Twagiramungu muwala wa Kayibanda.
Oluvannyuma ekibiina kya Social Democatic Party nakyo kyatandikibwawo.
Oluvannyuma wajjawo ekibiina kya Liberal Party ekikulemberwa Lando Ndasingwa, ng'ono ye Mutuusi yekka eyali mu kabineeti ya Habyarimana.
Ebibiina by'obufuzi ebyo byassa omukono ku ndagaano y'emirembe ey'e Arusha mu 1993.
Ebibiina ebyali bisinga amaanyi mu ebyo ebyassa omukono ku ndagaano eyo, ekya Habyarimana ekiyitibwa Republic Democratic Movement n'ekyo ekiyitibwa Rwandan Patriotic Front byali bya kutwala ebitundu 40 ku buli kikumi eky'ebifo mu gavumenti.
Okusinziira ku byafaayo by'eby'obufuzi bya Rwanda mu kiseera ekyo, Habyarimana ye yali omulabe omukulu ow'ebibiina by'obufuzi.
Okuva bwe kiri nti Habyarimana yalina obuyinza ku magye, engeri yokka ey'okuvuganya Habyarimana kwali kukola mukago na kibiina kya Rwandan Patriotic Front kubanga nakyo kyalina obuyinza obumala ku ggye nga kisobola okumulwanyisa.
Bwe kityo, ekibiina kya Republican Democratic Movement, ekya Social Democratic Party, n'ekya Liberal Party  byatuuka ku nzikiriziganya n'ekibiina kya Rwandan Patriotic Front okukolera awamu.
Omukago ogwo gwakyusa nnyo eby'obufuzi mu Rwanda.
Habyarimana yakiraba nti omukago gw'ebibiina bino gwali gugenda kuleetera ekibiina kye okuba n'ebifo bitonoko mu gavumenti.
Ebibiina gamba ng'ekya Republican Democratic Movement byali biraba nti olw'okuba RPF yalimu ab'eggwanga ly'Abatuusi bangi, ate ng'Abahutu balina obuyinza bungi, RPF yali tesobola kuwangula kulonda okwali kujja.
Baakiraba nti singa bakozesa obuyinza RPF bwe yalina ku magye ne babugattako amaanyi amatono ge baalina baali basobola okuwangula.
Naye ye Habyarimana ne banne bannalukalala ebintu baali babiraba bulala.
Baakiraba nti RPF yali egenda kuwangula ng'eyitira mu kwekobaana n'ebibiina by'obufuzi eby'Abahutu.
Okukwatagana wakati wa RPF n'ebibiina by'obufuzi ebirala byawa essuubi nti kati Abatuusi baali basobola okutwala obuyinza.
Habyarimana yasala amagezi amalala.
Ekisooka, yassaawo ekibiina kya Coalition for the Defence of the Republic, nga kino kyalimu Abatuusi bannalukalala.
Ab'ekibiina kya Coalition for the Defence of the Republic baali bagamba nti ensi ya Rwanda ya Bahutu bokka.
Mu kusooka, ab'ekibiina kya Coalition for the Defence of the Republic kyagaana endagaano y'e Arusha era tekyarowoozebwako mu ngabana y'obuyinza.
Naye bwe baakiraba  nti eyo tewaali lugendo, ab'ekibiina kya Coalition for the Defence of the Republic  ekyali kiwagirwa Habyarimana baatandika okusaba nabo bateekebwe mu ndagaano eyo.
Ekigendererwa kyali kya kunafuya maanyi ga mukago gwa RPF n'ebibiina ebirala.
Eky'okubiri, Habyarimana yafuba okuleetawo enjawukana mu bibiina by'obufuzi ebirala.
N'ekyavaamu, bannalukalala abaali mu bibiina ebyo baasalawo okwegatta ku Habyarimana ate abo abaagala okukwata ebintu obulungi baanywerera ku RPF.
Emirundi etaano, embiranyi eyo eyaliwo yakaandaaliriza eky'okukwasa gavumenti ey'awamu obuyinza, era embeera yali bw'etyo okuva mu Ddesemba 1993 okutuuka mu Apuli 1994 Habyarimana bwe yattibwa.
Kati okusinziira ku byali mu bukwakulizo obw'okussa wansi eby'okulwanyisa, RPF yawalirizibwa okuva mu bifo bye yali ewambye n'eddayo mu bifo bye yalimu ng'okulwana tekunnatandika mu Maayi 1993.
Ebifo RPF mwe yava byalangirirwa nti tebirina kubaamu magye era nti byali wansi w'ekibiina ky'Amawanga Amagatte ekyategeka okulonda mu Rwanda.
Wadde ng'ebibiina byonna byali bikkirizibwa okwenyigiramu, ekibiina kya Republican Democratic Movement n'ekya RPF bye byokka ebyasimbawo abantu.

Ebyo ebyaliwo byakiraga nti akakodyo Abahutu ke baali bakozesa kaali keetaaga okukyusibwa.
Baali basobodde okuleetera Abatuusi ab'amaanyi n'aba bulijjo okulowooza nti Abatuusi tebaggwana kufuga Rwanda.
Baakiraba nti singa tewabaawo kittabantu, kaweefube gwe baaliko ow'okuleetawo enjawukana ez'enkalakkalira wakati w'Abahutu n'Abatuusi yali ajja kugwa butaka.
N'olwekyo, ekittabantu tekyava ku kuba nti waaliwo obukyayi obwali buvudde edda wakati w'Abatuusi n'Abahutu.
Singa abo baali batumbula endowooza nti Abahutu be balina okufuga baali bakakafu nti Abahutu n'Abatuusi tebasobola kukola mukago, bandibadde tebasala ggezi ddala.
Kati olwo lwaki Abahutu aba bulijjo bangi baakwata ebijambiya okutta Abatuusi abaali mikwano gyabwe, baliraanwa baabwe, era nga babalinako oluganda?
Abantu bangi balowooza nti Abahutu bangi baasalawo okutta Abatuusi olw'okuba baabalinako obukyayi.
Abaali emabega w'ekittabantu baagamba nti Omuhutu yenna ateenyigira mu kittabantu yali ajja kuttibwa.
Eky'okubiri, Abahutu bangi baagambibwa nti singa Abatuusi bajja, bajja kutta Abahutu babasaanyeewo.
N'olwekyo, Abahutu bangi baasalawo okwenyigira mu kittabantu nga balowooza nti beetaasa.
N'olwekyo, ekittabantu tekyava ku kuba nti waaliwo obukyayi wakati w'Abatuusi n'Abahutu obwali buvudde emabega.

Mu kuwaayo okusaba kwe mu kkooti ensukulumu, Dr. Besigye yali ayagala okulonda kuddibwemu, ng'era ekibiina kya Museveni bwe kyali kyagala mu 1980.
Enjawulo yokka eriwo eri nti Museveni teyagenda mu kkooti.
Oluvannyuma yasalawo kugenda mu nsiko okuyeekera gavumenti.
Embeera y'ab'oludda oluvuganya gavumenti mu1980 efaananako n'eyo eriwo leero.
Ekibiina kya Museveni kyemulugunya nti gavumenti yali ekiremesa okukozesa emikutu gy'empuliziganya.
Leero, emikutu gy'empuliziganya mingi nnaddala leediyo ne TV gigaana okuwa olukusa ab'oludda oluvuganya nnaddala Besigye okugikozesa nga gigamba nti gifunye “ebiragiro okuva eri gavumenti."
Engeri gavumenti gy'etulugunyamu ab'oludda oluvuganya gavumenti efaanana n'engeri gavumenti gye yatulugunyaamu ab'oludda oluvuganya mu 1980.
Olupapula lwa Independent, Jjlaayi 23 - 29, 2010 byawandikibwa Mubatsi Asinja Habati ku ssaawa 4:30 ez'oku makya.
Samuel Bukawa, 57, alindirira mu kifo awatuukirwa abagenyi ku NSSF asobole okulaba oyo akola ku ssente eziterekebwa.
Bukawa atudde ku ntebe mu kifo awatuukirwa abagenyi nga yeesunga okufuna ssente z'amaze emyaka 16 ng'atereka.
Ng'abantu beeyongera okuyingira mu ofiisi ya NSSF, Bukawa, amaze eddakiika ezisukka mu 20 ng'alindirira, antunulira ng'alinga ayagala okuyomba.
Okusinziira ku mateeka ga NSSF, abakozi abaterekayo ssente bagwana okuweebwa ssente zaabwe singa baba baweza emyaka 50, nga bafunye obulemu obw'olubeerera, oba nga bagenda okuva mu ggwanga lubeerera.
Omuntu asobola okusaba ssente z'ow'enganda ze eyafa bw'aba nga ye yali abalabirira.
Kyokka, okumala emyaka 3, Bukawa tasobodde kufuna ku ssente obukadde 30 z'amaze ebbanga ng'atereka mu kitongole kya NSSF.
Leero, talina mulimu gumusasula bulungi ssente naye alina abantu mwenda ab'okulabirira.
Nga Jjulaayi 7, akakiiko ka paliyamenti kaakunya ekitongole kya NSSF olw'okubulankanya ssente z'abantu.
Kyazuulibwa nti nga 2007 ekitongole kya NSSF kyafiirwa obukadde bwa ssente obuwerako olw'abakozi baakyo okugingirira ebiwandiiko ne bafuna ssente mu lukujjukujju.
Wakkati wa Ddesemba 2007 ne Agusito 2008 NSSF yapangisa Freddie Egesa, omunoonyereza akulira ekitongole ky'obwannannyini ekya Global Equity Services Uganda Limited.
Egesa yakizuula nti ekitongole kya NSSf kyali kibbibwa ssente obukadde 200 buli luvannyuma lw'ennaku 90.
Yagamba nti abakozi ba NSSF baali bagingirira ebiwandiiko mu mannya g'abantu abamu be baasasulanga ssente.
Oluvannyuma lw'okunoonyereza okumala emyezi 8, Egesa yawa obujulizi ku bye yali azudde.
Yagamba nti yakizuula nti abakozi ba NSSF baali bagingiridde ebiwandiiko eby'okusasulirako abantu ssente eziwerera ddala obukadde 800.
Egesa yagamba nti, “Ssente ezo zeesiba abakozi abo bwe baalemererwa okuzisa mu bbanka."
Ekitongole kya NSSF ekyateekebwawo mu 1967, kye kitongole kyokka ekitereka ssente z'abakozi abatali ba gavumenti.
Ekyo kiri kityo kubanga abakozi abatali ba gavumenti tebafuna pensoni.
Singa etteeka erikwata ku bakozi abaawummula okufuna ssente erikubaganyizibwako ebirowoozo riyisibwa, guno gwe gujja okuba omulundi ogusooka mu Uganda abakozi okufuna eddembe ly'okwesalirawo.
Abakozi bajja kuba basobola okusalawo okutereka ssente mu NSSF, ekitongole kya gavumenti, oba mu kitongole ky'obwannannyini.
Kaabineeti yasemba etteeka eryo mu Ddesemba 2009 era lirindirirwa kukubaganyizibwako birowoozo mu paliyamenti.
Lyakuyamba mu kuleetawo ebitongole ebirala ebivuganya n'ekitongole kya NSSF kibe nga si kye kyokka ekitereka ssente z'abakozi, ekijja okutumbula obuweereza obuweebwa abakozi abaawummula.
Etteeka eryo era lyetaagisa wassibwewo ekitongole ekitalina kyekubiira okukakasa nti ssente z'abakozi zikwatibwa bulungi mu ggwanga.
Ensangi zino, ekitongole kya NSSF kitereka bulungi ssente z'abakozi awatali kuyingirirwa bannabyabufuzi era kituusa obuweereza obulungi ku bantu olw'okuvuganya okwajjawo.
Ekitongole ekyo kijja kuba kirabirira ebitongole bya gavumenti n'eby'obwannannyini ebikola ku pensoni.
Etteekaa lyetaagisa ebitongole ebigaba pensoni okuba n'ekitongole ekikola okunoonyereza n'okuwa abo ababiterekamu ssente amagoba agawerako.
Likugira eky'okussa ssente mu bintu ebitakakasibwa okuggyako okuzissa mu bintu gamba nga bbanka.
Omuntu ayagala okussaawo ekitongole ekitereka ssente z'abakozi alina omutemwa gwa ssente z'alina okusooka okuwaayo nga tannaweebwa layisinsi.
Ebitongole ebiriwo ebifugibwa Capital Market Authority nabyo bijja kwetaaga okufuna layisinsi empya.
Enkyukakyuza empya ezikwata ku pensoni zijja kutandika okukola mu 2011.
Nga Jjulaayi 23 - 29, 2010, olupapula lwa Independent lwafulumya okunoonyereza okulaga engeri etteeka epya gye linaakwata ku bitongole ebitereka ssente z'abakozi. 
Bwe yali atongoza akakiiko ka NSSF akapya omwaka oguwedde, minisita w'eby'ensimbi Syda Bbumba yagamba nti obutakola bulungi mirimu gyakyo kyali kiremessezza ekitongole ekyo okuwa abantu empeereza ey'omutindo.
Yagamba nti kabineeti yasemba eky'okulambika obulungi entambuza y'emirimu mu bitongole ebitereka ssente z'abakozi n'okukkiriza ebitongole ebirala okukola omulimu ogwo.
Yagattako nti ekyo kyali tekijja kusuula kitongole kya NSSF mu buzibu okuggyako ng'abakikulira balemeddwa okukola ekibasuubirwamu.
Enkyukakyuka ezo zijja kuwa abakozi n'ababakozesa akakisa okwesalirawo kitongole ki ekinaabaterekera ssente zaabwe era kijja kusobozesa abakozi okuganyulwa mu ssente ze batereka n'okuzifunamu amagoba.
Ebitongole ebirala nabyo bijja kukkirizibwa okutereka ssente z'abakozi era kijja kuba eri ababiddukanya n'abalala ababivunaanyizibwako okukakasa  nti bikola bulungi emirimu gyabyo.
Ibrahim Okumu, omukugu mu by'enfuna mu yunivasite y'e Makerere, agamba nti, “Okukkiriza n'ebitongole ebirala okutereka ssente z'abakozi kirungi nnyo.”.
Ibrahim Okumu yagattako nti, “Kijja kuleeta ba invesita abalala abanaaleetawo okuvuganya okusingako ."
Akatale k'eby'ensimbi mu Uganda okusingira ddala kasinziira ku muwendo gwa ba invesita abeetegefu okuteresebwa ssente okumala ebbanga ddene.
Yeeyongera n'agamba nti, “Mu kiseera kino, ekitongole kya NSSF kye kyokka ekisobola okutereka ssente z'abantu okumala ebbanga ddene n'okuzissa mu bizineesi ezikola amagoba."
Yagattako nti, "Kino tekijja kukoma ku kwongera ku ssente ezisobola okuteekebwa mu bizineesi naye era kijja kwongera ku nkulaakulana ya Uganda."
Okumu alowooza nti enkola ya NSSF ey'okuwa abakozi amagoba amatono ku ssente zaabwe, ejja kukyuka olw'okuvuganya okugenda okujjawo.
Agamba nti, “Okuleetera NSSF okulekera awo okwefuga akatale kijja kuleetawo okuvuganya okw'amaanyi mu bitongole ebiteresi bya ssente z'abakozi ekijja okutumbula empeereza era kisikirize abakozi bangi okutereka ssente zaabwe mu bitongole ebyo.”
Okumu yeeyongera n'agamba nti, “Tusuubira nti kati wajja kubaawo okwegendereza nga ssente tezinnateekebwa mu kintu kyonna ekizza amagoba era nti abakozi bajja kufuna amagoba agasingako ku ssente zaabwe ze bateresezza."
Kyokka, Kiwanuka Kunsa, eyeebuuzibwako mu nsonga z'ebitongole ebiteresi bya ssente z'abakozi, agamba nti enkola eno empya eyaniriziddwa naye wakyaliwo ebyebuuzibwa ku ngeri gy'eneetambulamu .
Olumu kyali kitwalibwa ng'obukakafu obulabwako obulaga nti Uganda efaayo nnyo ku banoonyi b'obubudamo.
Naye kati ebyo ebyali mu nkambi y'e Nakivale n'ey'e Kyaka biyinza okuwa ekifaananyi ekirala ku Uganda.
Nga Jjulaayi 14, ekitongole kya poliisi mu Ugandan nga kikolera wamu n'ab'obuyinza mu Rwanda beekwasa ensonga ezitaali ntuufu ne bakwata Abanyarwanda abanoonyi b'obubudamo nga 2,000 era ne babazzaayo ku kifuba mu nsi yaabwe.
Ekikwekweto ekyo, ekyavumirirwa ennyo ekitongole ky'ensi yonna ekikola ku banoonyi b'obubudamu n'abalwanirizi b'eddembe ly'obuntu , byaleka abanoonyi b'obubudamo babiri nga bafudde ate abalala 26 ne bagendera ku bisago.
Abanoonyi b'obubudamo abo baali bagezaako okubuuka ku loole eyali ebasaza ensalo okubazzaayo e Rwanda.
Ku Lwokusatu kumakya, abasirikale ba poliisi bangi nga bali wamu n'abasirikale ba Rwanda beebungulula enkambi ezo ebbiri.
Abasirikale ba Rwanda abo baasendasenda abanoonyi b'obubudamo okukungaana nga babalimba nti bagenda kubawa mmere n'okubalambululira engeri gye bayinza okujuliramu.
Amasasi gaakubwa mu bbanga okulabula abanoonyi b'obubudamo abaali bagaanye okulinnya loole ezibazzaayo e Rwanda  nga poliisi bwe yali ebalagidde.
Abanoonyi b'obubudamu 2,000 kati bakuumirwa mu bifo ebitali bya nkalakkalira mu Rwanda.
Ate abo 26 abaafuna ebisago bakyali mu Uganda era bajjanjjabirwa mu bulwaliro obuli okumpi ne Nakivale.
Mu myaka esatu egiyise, gavumenti ya Rwanda eyongedde amaanyi mu kuggya abanoonyi b'obubudamo Abanyarwanda mu mawanga agali ku muliraano omuli Uganda ne Tanzania, bazzibweyo e Rwanda.
Ekikwekweto eky'amaanyi ekyasooka okukolebwa okuzzaayo ku mpaka abanoonyi b'obubudamu mu nsi yaabwe kyakolebwa nga Okitobba 3, 2007, abanoonyi b'obubudamo 3,000 Abanyarwanda bwe bazzibwayo mu nsi yaabwe.
Ekikwekweto ekyo kyakolebwa poliisi n'abantu abalala abaalina eby'okulwanyisa abaazingako obusiisira bw'abanoonyi b'obubudamo ku ssaawa 8:00 ez'ekiro ng'ekitongole ky'ensi yonna ekikola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamu kiraba.
Okusinziira ku mukungu omu akola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamo, Salima Namusobya, yagamba nti ebikwekweto ng'ebyo tebitera kubaawo era nti bikolebwa gavumenti ya Rwanda ng'ekolagana wamu n'eya Uganda.
Emyaka bwe gizze gitambula, ekibiina ekikola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamu mu nsi yonna kibadde kifuna enkungaana n'ab'obuyinza mu Ugandan ne Rwanda ku nsonga z'okuzzaayo Abanyarwanda mu nsi yaabwe.
Mu Rwanda, abanoonyi b'obubudamo bakuumirwa mu bifo ebimu okumala akaseera katono naye nga bwe bamala okuteebwa era banoonya engeri gye baddayo e Uganda.
Olw'okuba baba tebakyabaagala, abanoonyi b'obubudamo abo babazzaayo misinde nga bayitira ku nsalo eri okumpi n'enkambi y'e Kyangwali okumpi n'akabuga k'e Hoima.
Mu kifaananyi ekimu ekyafulumira mu lupapula lwa Independent olwa Jjulaayi 23 - 29, 2010, kyagambibwa nti abanoonyi b'obubudamu bwe bakomawo e Uganda tebeemanyisa eri ba buyinza mu Uganda. 
Era tebeemanyisa eri kitongole ekikola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamu mu nsi yonna, mu kifo ky'ekyo babulira mu byalo ebiriranye enkabi ezo mu bugwanjuba bwa Uganda.   
Nabusobya agamba nti, “Abasinga obungi ku banoonyi b'obubudamo abazzibbwayo mu 2007 baakomawo dda.”
Nabusobya agattako nti, “Bangi ku Banyarwanda abazzibwayo ku kifuba bakomawo ne beewandiisa ng'abanoonyi b'obubudamo Abakongo era ekyo kiba tekiyambye mawanga gombi gazingirwamu."
Naye Kai Nielsen, akiikirira ekitongole ky'ensi yonna ekikola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamu mu Uganda, yalina kye yeebuuza. 
Abamu ku abo abazzibwayo nga Jjulaayi 14, mwe mwali n'abo abaali batannagaanibwa ddala kufuna bubudamo mu Uganda.
Obujulizi obwaweebwa ab'enganda z'abantu abo mu nkambi bulaga nti baali bakkiriziddwa okubeera mu ggwanga ng'abanoonyi b'obubudamo.
Naye abantu abo awamu n'abo abaali baajulira be bamu ku abo abazzibwayo ku kifuba e Rwanda.
Nielsen era yagamba nti kyewuunyisa nnyo okuba nti poliisi ya Rwanda yajja okukolera emirimu gyayo mu Uganda.
Kati okumala ekiseera, gavumenti ya Rwanda ebaddenga egamba nti Abanyarwanda tekikyabeetaagisa kuddukira mu nsi ndala yonna nga banoonyi ba bubudamo.
Wadde nga Uganda ekyakkiriza abanoonyi b'obubudamo okuyingira eggwanga, mu mwaka oguwedde yagaana Abanyarwanda ebitundu 98 ku buli kikumi okufuna obubudamo mu ggwanga.
Abanyarwanda bangi abanoonyi b'obubudamo baava mu Rwanda ne baddukira mu Uganda olw'ekittabantu ekyali mu Rwanda mu 1994, naye kati gye buvuddeko abantu badduka mu Rwanda lwa nsonga za bya bufuzi.
Ab'ekitongole kya Refugee Law Project bakizudde nti Abanyarwanda bangi batya okuddayo mu Rwanda olw'okutya okutulugunyizibwa.
Namusobya yagamba nti, “Abanoonyi b'obubudamu bano bwe baddayo, batulugunyizibwa, ate abalala tebabaddiza bintu byabwe.”
Abo abakomawo e Uganda bagamba nti abantu mu gavumenti bezza ettaka lyabwe era nti ebitongole by'abanoonyi b'obubudamo mu Rwanda tebikola kimala kubayamba.
Ekitongole ekirwanirira eddembe ly'obuntu kigamba nti wadde ng'ekitongole ekiramuzi mu Rwanda kirongoose okusinga bwe kyali mu 2004, tewannabaawo bukakafu bumala bulaga nti omuntu asobola okulamulwa mu mazima n'obwenkanya.
Ate era wabaddewo okulinnyirira eddembe ly'obuntu mu Rwanda, omuli okutiisatiisa abantu n'okutulugunya bannabyabufuzi naddala mu biseera by'okulonda pulezidenti okwaliwo nga Agusito 9.
Nielsen yeebuuza ensonga lwaki Uganda yakolagana ne Rwanda mu kuzzaayo abanoonyi b'obubudamu ku kifuba.
Yagamba nti, “Nze siraba nsonga lwaki bakaka abantu bano okuddayo mu Rwanda.”
Era yagamba nti, “Sikiwa nti abantu bano baali ba bulabe eri gavumenti ya Uganda oba nti yali tesobola kubalabirira."
Minisita w'ebigwa bitalaze Tarsis Kabwegye yagaana okukkiriza nti abanoonyi b'obubudamo bawalirizibwa okuddayo mu nsi zaabwe.
Yagamba nti abo abazzibwayo baali badduse lwa nsonga za byabufuzi era nti gavumenti ya Rwanda erina eddembe okujja n'etwala abantu baayo "ababa basobeddwa nga tebamanyi kya kukola"
Naye ye Namusobya agamba nti abamu ku banoonyi b'obubudamo abo baali bagwana n'okuweebwa obutuuze mu Uganda.
Abanoonyi b'obubudamo bangi bamaze mu Uganda emyaka egisukka mu 20 era ssemateeka abakkiriza okufuna obutuuze, ate era Abanyarwanda abasinga obungi bayizeeyo waakiri olulimi lumu olwogerwa mu Uganda.
Wadde nga ssemateeka wa Uganda owa 2006 akkiriza abanoonyi b'obubudamu abamaze ebbanga eggere okufuna obutuuze, ekitongole kya Uganda ekikola ku nsonga z'abantu abayingira mu ggwanga kiremesa abanoonyi b'obubudamo okufuna obutuuze.  
Namusobya yagamba nti ekitongole kya Refugee Law Project kiteekateeka okuwaayo okusaba mu kkooti ekkirize abanoonyi b'obubudamo abamaze emyaka egisukka mu 20 mu Uganda okuweebwa obutuuze.
Abasinga obungi ku Bannyarwanda abo tebakyalina kakwate na nsi yaabwe era okubakaka okuddayo kiba tekibayamba n'akamu.
Abanoonyi b'obubuddamu bava ku loole mu nkambi y'e Matanda mu disitulikiti y'e Kanungu.
Abanoonyi b'obubuddamu bangi abazzibwayo e Rwanda ku mpaka bakomawo mu Uganda nga bagamba nti Bakongo.
Ekifaananyi ekyakubibwa mu Okitobba 2007, Uganda yazzaayo Abanyarwanda 3,000 e Rwanda mu kiro ky'Olwokusatu ab'obuyinza bwe baazingako enkambi y'e Kyaka II n'ey'e Nakivale. 
Mu kiro ekyo, Abanyarwanda nkumi na nkumi baagobebwa mu nkambi ezo mu ngeri ey'obukambwe.
Eyeerabirako n'agage yagamba bannamawulire nti abanoonyi b'obubuddamu baateekebwa ku Fuso nnya ne bakakibwa okugenda amatumbi budde.
Abantu beekalakaasa nga bawakanya eky'okumenya etteeka ery'Amawanga Amagatte erigaana okukkakka abantu okuddayo mu ggwanga lye baddukamu.
Mu kiseera ekyo, ekitongole ky'ensi yonna ekikola ku nsonga z'abanoonyi b'obubudamo kyakkiriza ebyo gavumenti ya Rwanda ne Uganda ze byakigamba nti abantu abo baddayo 'kyeyagalire'.  
Kigambibwa nti waaliwo n'abanoonyi b'obubuddamu abamu abaagezaako n'okwetta nga bakozesa eddagala ly'ente nga baagala okwewala okuzzibwayo e Rwanda.
Abanoonyi b'obubuddamu, ng'abamu baali basussa mu myaka 50 egy'obukulu, baakakibwa okuddayo mu Rwanda. 
Empapula z'amawulire zaagamba nti ebitundu ebyasinga okukosebwa ennyo by'ebyo ebyalimu Abanyarwanda Abahutu abangi abaasooka okubudamirako e Tanzania naye ne bagobwayo mu 2003.
Abanoonyi b'obubuddamu Abanyarwanda abasinga obungi bajja mu Uganda oluvannyuma lwa Tanzania okutandika okubazzaayo e Rwanda n'eryanyi.
Abanoonyi b'obubuddamu abasukka mu 5,000 bajja mu Uganda mu 2003.
Olupapula lwa Independent olwa July 23 - 29, 2010, fayiro eyakolebwa Rowan Emslie yalaga nti mu kiro obulumbaganyi obwo lwe bwakolebwa, buli omu yasigala mu ntiisa.  
Nnayogerako n'omwami n'omukyala omu abaali balabira omupiira ku bbaala eyitibwa The Lion’s Den, eriraanye Ethiopian Village Restaurant.           
Nga Kampala agenda adda mpolampola mu nteeko, enneewulira z'abantu mu kibuga nazo zigenda zikyuka. 
Abantu banyiivu olwa Al Shabaab okukola ekintu eky'ettima bwe kityo era banyiivu olwa poliisi obutakola kimala kwetegekera bulumbaganyi obwo, era bali mu kutya. 
Mu alipoota gye yakola, omwekenneenya omu ayitibwa John Mueller yagamba nti bwe wabaawo obulumbaganyi bw'abatujju, emirundi egisinga amawanga gakwata era ne gatulugunya abantu abatalina musango, oboolyawo nga basinziira ku byafaayo bye babalinako.
Ebyo ebikwata ku Russia ne Chechnya mu 1999 oba ebyaliwo nga Isirairi enoonya Abapalesitiina bikiraga bulungi.
Pulezidenti Museveni okusuubiza okusindika abasirikale abalala 20,000 mu Somalia yakyogeza busungu na lwa kwagala kulaga lyanyi.
Ebyo yabyogera oluvannyuma lw'omu ku bakulembera Al Shabaab okugamba nti obulumbaganyi obwo baabukola kwesasuza Uganda olw'okusindika amagye e Somaliya era nti eyo ntandikwa butandikwa.
Mueller amanyiddwa nnyo mu kunoonyereza ku nsonga za bannalukalala era agamba nti talaba nsonga lwaki okufa kw'abantu abatonotono kuviirako abantu okutta abantu bangi nnyo nga bagezaako okwesasuza.
Mu kitabo 'Reactions and Overreactions to Terrorism,’ Mueller agamba nti “wadde ng'abatujju batta abantu, omuwendo gw'abantu be batta buli mwaka mu nsi yonna okutwalira awamu mutono." 
Abanoonyereza babiri okuva mu Amerika, Jennifer Merolla ne Elizabeth Zechmeister, baamala emyaka etaano nga banoonyereza ku ngeri abantu okutwalira awamu gye batwalamu obulumbaganyi bwa bannalukalala era n'engeri abantu gye bakyusaamu endowooza yaabwe.
Ebikolwa eby'obukambwe ebikolebwa ku bantu b'eggwanga abatujju mwe baava byeraliikiriza, nnaddala bw'olowooza ku ky'okuba nti Uganda ebadde emanyiddwa ng'ensi omuntu mw'asobola okufunira emirembe.
Ate n'ekirala ekisinga okweraliikiriza kiri nti abantu tebaasanyukira tteeka paliyamenti lye yabaga wiiki ewedde erikwata ku kulumika amasimu.
Karin Bridger, omukwasi wa vidiyo akolera mu Uganda agamba nti abantu abamu bo basazeewo okuba n'endowooza egamba nti ‘sigala ng'oli mukkakkamu weeyongereyo n'obulamu' ate abalala bo okutya kubassannyalazza.
Abo abaagenda okukola ku Bbalaza nga  balinga abatafuddeeyo nnyo baasobera abantu abaali bakubiddwa entiisa olw'ekyo ekyali kibaddewo.
Munnamateeka omu ataayagala kwatuukirizibwa mannya yagamba nti oluvannyuma lw'obulumbaganyi obwo, ye yagenda ku mulimu ku Bbalaza. 
Omu ku bantu ataalemesa bulumbaganyi obwo kumusannyalaza yagamba nti, "Tekyetaagisa kweraliikirira kisukkiridde."
Era kigambibwa nti wabaawo obusungu n'okutya ebireetebwa ebintu ebitonotono ebiyinza okubaawo ennaku nga bbiri oba ssatu oluvannyuma.
Omusawo eyayitibwa okugenda e Mulago mu kiro ekyo nga bbomu zaakakuba abantu era eyakolera mu mbeera eyo ey'entiisa yagamba bw'ati.
Ng'ayogera ku ngeri y'okwaŋŋanga embeera oluvannyuma lw'obulumbaganyi obwaliwo nga Jjulaayi 11, Mueller, agamba nti talaba nsonga lwaki okufa kw'abantu abatonotono kuviirako abantu okutta abantu bangi nnyo nga bagezaako okwesasuza.

Suubi 2011 kibiina ekyegattirwamu bannabyabufuzi okuva mu bibiina eby'enjawulo, ate mu kiseera kye kimu ne beeyita aba DP.

Solomon Kimbugwe munnamawulire w'olupapula lwa independenti olwa Jjulaayi okuva nga 30 okutuuka nga Agusito 5 2010, yawandiika nti ekibiina kya CP kyali kirina omuntu atamanyiddwa gwe kyogeddeko ng'anaabakwatira bbendera avuganye n'abantu ababiri abeesimbyewo okuvuganya ku kifo kya pulezidenti.

Lukwago ne Namboozi baali beebuuza obanga "bakyewaggula" bannenyigira mu kusunsulibwa kw'ekibiina kya DP.
Tewaliwo nnyo kya maanyi kimanyiddwa ku Omukenkufu James Kigongo ku nsonga z'eby'obufuzi oba ku bikwata ku mirimu gye emirala okuggyako okuba nti olumu yakulemberako ekitongole mu Ssetendekero wa Makerere.
Ekifo ekisingayo okuba ekya waggulu kye yali abaddemu mu by'obufuzi kwe kuba nti yaliko omuwi w'amagezi wa pulezidenti wa CP Ken Lukyamuzi.
Kigongo yalondebwa mu kiseera kya ttabamiruka w'ekibiina kya CP eky'ababaka 60 abakiikirira ebitundu so si disitulikiti era kino kyaliwo mu Jjulaayi nga 23 e Kampala.
Yawangula Wasiebe Magina, omumyuka wa CP mu Buvanjuba n'obululu 32 ku obwo 60 obwakubibwa.
Oboolyawo ekintu ekisingayo obukulu ekikakasiddwa mu kulondebwa kwa Kigongo kwe kuba nti ekibiina kino kizimbiddwa ku musingi gwa federo.
Kimanyiddwa bulungi nti Kigongo awagira nnyo obwakabaka ne federo.
Kino kiba kiraga nti federo Buganda gy'esinga okutwala ng'ekikulu ennyo y'ejja okuba ku mwanjo mu kibiina kino ekigattira awamu ebibiina byonna.
Kyokka bw'oleeta Kigongo avuganye Besigye ne Otunu obanga eddidde ekibala kya appo n'emiyembe n'obiteeka mu kisero n'ogamba omuntu alondeko ky'asinga okwagala.
Kino kiba kyeyoleka kaati nti embiranye ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti okusinga ejja kuba wakati wa Besigye ne Otunnu.
Naye waliwo ensonga enkulu wadde nga si ya maanyi nnyo mu kulondebwa kwa Kigongo okukwattira ekibiina kya CP etaala.
Ebibiina by'obufuzi byonna bikikoze okuggyako ekya NRM.
Mu bbanga eritasukka myaka etaano UPC ekyusizza obukulembeze bwaayo ne buva ku Maria Obote ne budda ku Otunnu.
Maria Obute yalondebwa oluvannyuma lw'okufa kw'omwami we Milton Obote eyali akulemberera ekibiina kino mu buwaŋŋanguse.
Ng'oggyeko enjawukana eziri mu kibiina kya DP,  kyo kyakakyusa obukulembeze bwakyo emirundi ebiri bukya NRM ejja mu buyinza mu 1986
Ate kyo ekibiina kya FDC ekisngayo obuto mu bibiiina ebinene ebina era nga kyatandikibwawo mu 2004 nakyo kisuubirwa okukyusa obukulembeze bwakyo mu 2011.
Omukulembeze w'ekibiina kino Dr. Kizza Besigye yagamba nti tajja kuddamu kwesimbawo ng'ekisanja kye kiweddeko.
Mu bibiina byonna ebyakamala emyaka egisukka mu kkumi, ekibiina kya NRM kyokka kye kitakyusanga bukulembeze bwakyo obwoku ntikko.
Museveni y'abaddewo mu myaka 24 egiyise.
Museveni y'abadde ssentebe wa NRM okuviira ddala mu 1986 lwe yajja mu buyinza.
Eky'okugamba nti NRM yafuka ekibiina ky'eby'obufuzi mu 2003 naye nti okuva mu mwaka 1986 ebadde nkola ya mugendo, ebyo byo bigambo bugambo.
Mu 2002 kkooti ya ssemateeka yasalawo nti NRM kyali kibiina kya bya bufuzi wadde nga kyali kyefula okuba omugendo obugendo kubanga kyalina ssentebe na byonna ebikigwanyiza okuba ekibiina.

Mu mawulire ga Independent aga Jjulaayi 30 okutuuka ku Agusito 5, 2010 Ken Lukyamuzi yayogerwako mu kitundu ekikwata ku by'okulonda mu ggwanga.
Sam Serwanga yawandiika ku bukambwe obweyolekera mu kulonda wakati mu myaka gya 1980 ne 2011.
Mwami Nakendo ye mumyuka wa ssentebe w'akakiiko k'amagye.
Nakendo yagamba nti "Yoweri Museveni talina magye gage ku bubwe."
Museveni nga pulezidenti w'ekibiina ky'eby'obufuzi ekiyitibwa UPM, ekimu ku bibiina ebina ebivuganya mu kulondebwa okunaabaawo ku Lwokusatu olujja, kigambibwa nti alina eggye ly'addumira era ly'atendeka. 
Bino byayogerwa Paul Muwanga ssentebe w'akakiiko k'amagye mu lukuŋŋaana lwa UPC olwali e Kashongi mu Nyabushozi ekitundu Museveni gy'asibuka.
Muwanga amaze ennaku omukaaga ng'alambula ebitundu eby'omukyalo era ng'akuba enkuŋŋaana z'ekibiina kya UPC mu Mpigi, Masaka ne Mbarara, yawa okulabula eri Dr. Bernard Buzabo.
Dr. Buzabo era nga ye mumyuka wa minisita w'eby'obulunzi n'obuvubi yakubirizibwa okulekera awo eby'obufuzi ebirumba abalala era ebirimu ekigendererwa eky'okutiisatiisa abawagizi ba UPC mu Mbarara.
Museveni yakyogera kaati nti ye yali talina ggye lirye ku bubwe era nti talina ggye lyonna ly'atendeka.
Naye singa wabaawo omuntu yenna atendeka eggye erirye ku bubwe, eggye eryo teriyiza kusinga eggye lya Uganda ennunuzi ate nga lye ggye lyammwe.

Nga babbira ekibiina kya NRM.
Baagala wabeewo akakiiko akeetengeredde akanaateekateeka okulonda nga keesigamiziddwa ku nkalala z'abalonzi abatuufu.
Ekibiina kino ekyegattirwamu bannabyabufuzi okuva mu bibiina ebitali bimu tekakkiriziganya na nkalala z'abalonzi ezaategekebwa akakiiko k'eby'okulonda.
Mu lukuŋŋana lw'abamawulire olwaliwo nga 4 ku kitebe ekikulu eky'akakiiko k'eby'okulonda era ng'olukuŋŋaana nga luno lubaawo buli wiiki, oyo akola nga ssentebe yawa ekirango.
Joseph Biribonwa yagamba nti baali bazudde mu lukalala lw'abalonzi abantu 159,419 abaali beewandisizza emirundi ebiri oba n'okusingawo.
Abantu obukadde kkumi na butaano mu emitwalo abiri mu musanvu be balonzi abeewandiisa mu bantu abateeberezebwa okuba obukadde amakumi asatu mu bubiri abali mu Uganda.
Ng'oggyeko eky'okuteeka akazito ku bikwata ku nkyukakyuka erina okukolebwa mu by'okulonda, okufuna emikono akakadde kamu nakyo kijja kwongera okuleeta abawagizi mu kibiin ky'eby'obufuzi kino ekyegattirwamu bannabyafuzi okuva mu bibiina ebitali bimu.
Margret Wokuri, omukwanaganya w'ekibiina ekirwanirira wabeewo okulonda okw'amazima n'obwenkanya yagamba nti ebinaavaamu bijja kuba birungi nnyo.
Ingrid Turinawe yakubiriza ebibiina ebiralala okubeegattako mu lutalo luno olw'okulwanirira okulonda okw'amazima n'obwenkanya.
Kimaze okufuna abawagizi okuva mu bibiina eby'enjawulo gamba nga ekyo eky'abavubuka abava mu bibiina eby'enjawulo, ekyo ekirwanirira wabeewo okulonda okw'amazima n'obwenkanya era n'ekya Suubi.
Turinawe agamba nti okulwanagana okw'amaanyi okwaliwo wiiki ewedde mu kusunsulibwa kw'ekibiina kya NRM kulaga bulazi nti ekibiina kino kirimu ebikolwa eby'obukambwe.

Tuwakanya obutuufu bw'omusango guno mu kkooti ya ssemateeka.
Ab'omu maka ga Rukiya Makumaamin balina okubaako akamyenyumyenyu okuvira ddala awaka okutuuka ku bbanka.
Ab'omu maka ga eyaliko pulezidenti wa Uganda Idi Amin bannatera okwefunira omudidi gwa bukadde kikumi obwa ddola olw'omulimu omwekusifu ogwakolebwa.
Yakwanaganya omulimu guno ne Yasser Arafat eyali pulezidenti wa Palesitina mu myaka gya 1970.
Mutabani wa Amini ayitibwa Jafari Amini akikakasizza nti ab'omu maka gaabwe baluubirira okufuna sente ezo nga bayambibwako abalangira b'e Saudi.
Ssente ezo zaali kirabo ekyaweebwa Amini olw'okusalawo okuwa Abawarabu ekitiibwa kye yali awa Abaisirayiri.
Mu kusooka Amini yali munywanyi wa Isirairi era nga bano be baamuyamba okummamulako Obote mu Jjanwali 1971.
Kyokka, oluvannyuma Amin yakyusa endowooza ye mu by'obufuzi era mu Jjuuni 1972 yakyalira amawanga ga Buwarabu agatali gamu era n'abagamba nga kati bw'akolagana nabo mu kifo kya Yisirayiri.

Awatali kubuusabuusa, pulezidenti Kagame yawangula okulonda okwo.
Mu kiseera ekitali kya wala olupapula lw'amawulire olwa Independenti lujja kukyaza Jimmy n'ekigendererwa eky'okukubaganya ebirowoozo.
Ekigendererwa kye ky'okwongera okunyweza obukuumi eri abantu oluvannyuma lwa bbomu aba Al-Shabaab ze baatulisizza e Kampla mu Jjulaayi nga 11.
Mu Uganda temukyalimu eyaliko pulezidenti era wajja kuyitawo ekiseera kiwanvu nga tewannabaawo mulala.
Godfrey Binaisa abadde akyasigaddewo ku abaaliko ba pulezidenti naye yafa wiiki ewedde.
Binaisa yafuga Uganda okuva Jjuuni nga 20, 1979 okutuuka Maayi 1980.
Akakiiko k'amagye akakulemberwa Paulo Muwanga era nga Yoweri Museveni ye mummyuka waako, kaamummamula ku ntebe mu Maayi nga 12, 1980.

Ekibiina kya NRM kyenyigidde mu bikolwa eby'obukambwe ebirimu okukuba amasasi, okusindikagana n'okulumiriziganya olw'okugulirira abalonzi awamu n'ebikolwa ebirala ebibi. 
Ebikyasinze okubeerera ddala ebibi byebyo ebyali mu disitulikiti y'e Sembabule wiiki ewedde nga bikwata ku Theodore Sekikubo ow'e Lwemiyaga ne Sam Kuteesa ow'e Mawogola.

Bbanka y'ensi yonna awamu n'abagabirizi b'obuyambi abalala nga 9, baawa okulabula okw'amaanyi bwe baasala ku buyambi bwe bawa Uganda ebitundu kkumi ku buli kikumi.
Kino kyakolebwa kubanga gavumenti ya Uganda yali eremereddwa okukola ku buli bw'enguzi obukudde eggyembe.
Abagabirizi b'obuyambi baali bategese okuwa Uganda ensimbi ezibalirwa mu ddoola z'Amerika obukadde 360 mu mwaka gw'eby'ensimbi 2010/2011.
Kino kyayogerwa abo abavunaanyizibwa ku kuwa Uganda obuyambi.
Nga mu bano mwe muli Banka ey'ensi yonna, omukago gwa Bulaaya, Austrelia, Bubirigi, Denmark, German, Ireland, Norway, Netherlands, Sweden ne Bungereza.
Baagamba nti baatuuka ku kusalawo okukola kino oluvannyuma lw'okwetegeereza engeri gavumenti gye yakolamu mu mwaka gw'eby'ensimbi ogwa 2008/2009, ogwafundikirwa mu 2010.
Abagabirizi b'obuyambi banyiivu nnyo olwa gavumenti okulemererwa okubaako eky'amaanyi ky'ekolawo ku misango gy'obuli bw'enguzi mu mwaka 2008/2009.
Okusingira ddala emisango egyo gyegyo egyayogerwako mu alipoota y'olukuŋŋaana lw'abakulembeze b'amawanga agali mu lusse olumu ne Bungereza eya 2008 ekwata ku by'embalirira.
Mu bbanga erisukka omwaka omulamba oluvannyuma lw'alipoota eyo okufulumizibwa, abagabirizi b'obuyambi bagamba nti tewaliwo kya maanyi kikoleddwa.
Mu mwaka gw'eby'ensimbi ogwa 2008/2009, obuyambi obuva ebweru bwali ebitundu asatu ku buli kikumi mu mbalirira y'eggwanga.

Otunnu naye si muntu mwangu.
Mu lupapula lw'amawulire olwa Independenti olwa Agusito nga 13 okutuuka nga 19, Andrew Mwenda yawandiika.
Mu kyeya kya 1995, Jimmy Carter eyaliko pulezidenti w'Amerika yateekateeka olukuŋŋaana mu kibuga Tunis nga lukwata ku Rwanda.
Ekigendererwa ky'olukuŋŋaana olwo kwali okumatiza gavumenti ya Rwanda okussaawo kabineeti ey'ekintabuli nga mulimu ne bannabyabufuzi Abahutu.
Mu lukuŋŋaana olwo mwalimu baliraanwa ba Rwanda gamba nga pulezidenti wa Zaire Mobutu Sese Seko, owa Uganda Yoweri Museveni n'owa Tanzania Ali Hassan Mwinyi.
Mwalimu ne pulezidenti wa Rwanda Pasteur Bizimungu awamu ne eyaliko pulezidenti wa Tanzaniya Julius Nyerere.
Bwe baali nga banywa ku kakyayi, balina bye baayogerako ne Carter.
Eyaliko pulezidenti wa Amerika yabuuza Bizimungu ensonga lwaki tabaako Abahutu b'alonda okubeera ku kabineeti.
Bizimungu yasaba Carter ekibuuzo ekyo akibuuze Nyerere.
Carter yabuuza Julius nti, "Lwaki gavumenti ya Rwanda terondayo waakiri omu ku Bahutu n'abeera ku kabineeti?"
Nyerere yaddamu mu ngeri ye ey'okujeregerera nti: "Nze siddamu bibuuzo bikwata ku mawanga".
Julius yagattako nti buuza Mobutu wuuwo okuva bwe kiri nti ye kakensa w'eby'obufuzi ebyawula mu mawangaa.
Carter ng'atabuddwa, yakyukira ensolo enkambwe ey'omu Afirika.
Ow'ekitiibwa pulezidenti, awo n'atunuulira Mobutu mu maaso, "lwaki mu kabineeti ya Rwanda temuli bannabyabufuzi Abahutu?"
Ssabaminisita Faustin Twagiramungu naye Muhutu.
Abanyarwanda abalala abaali batudde awo ku mmeeza ne batandika okunokolayo abalala, era amangu ago ne bakola olukalala lwa baminisita ne baluwa Carter.
Ebitundu ebisukka mu nkaaga ku buli kikumi baali baminisita Abahutu.
Carter yawuniikirira nnyo era n'akyukira abakulembeze abalala bonna n'ababuuza nti: "Kati olwo olukuŋŋaana luno lwaki?"
Kino kigendereddwamu okukubaganya ebirowoozo ku Rwanda ku mikutu gy'amawulire egy'e Bulaaya naye ng'okusingira ddala kikanga abali mu Afirika.
Okumala ebyesa n'ebyasa kibadde kyogerwa nti Abahutu n'Abatusi tebaagalanira ddala.
Obulimba ng'obwo obuli mu byafaayo bwe busiize enziro ku by'obufuzi bwa Rwanda.
Tewaliiwo biwandiiko ebikwata ku Rwanda ng'abafuzi b'amatwale tebannajja biraga nti Abatusi n'Abahutu babaddenga tebaagalana.
Mu butuufu n'ebyafaayo ebikwata ku bulabe obwasimba amakanda mu mawanga g'omu Afirika kitundu ku bulimba buno.
Bino byonna byasavuwazibwa omuntu omu okuva mu Bulaaya mu kyasa ekya 19.
Eby'obufuzi bya Afirika ebyesigamiziddwa ku njawukana mu mawanga si bikadde nga bw'olaba essimu ezikolebwa ate ne ziddamu okukolebwa buli lunaku.
Kale tekyewuunyisa nti okusinziira ku kunoonyereza okwakolebwa mu 2009 kyazuulibwa nti enjawukana mu mawanga okusinga eri abo abatwalibwa okuba abagezi ennyo okusinga bw'eri mu bantu aba wansi.
Eky'ennaku kiri nti abagezi bangi mu Afirika batwala endowooza y'abazungu okuba nti ye ntuufu.
Tebakimanyi nti amawanga agamu agasinga obunene mu ssemazinga waffe gamba nga Abakyukuyu n'Abayoruba gaatondebwawo abafuzi b'amatwale.
Naye kasita gaamala okutondebwawo ne gatandika okugoberera empisa ezaabwe ku bwabwe.
Ng'ekyokulabirako, gye buvuddeko awo gavumenti ya Rwanda yakyusa erinnya ly'ekitta bantu okuva ku "Kitta bantu ekyali e Rwanda" ne liba "Ekitta abatuusi."
Olw'okuba baakola kinene okukomya ekitta bantu, gavumenti ya Rwanda yeyongedde okukozesa ekitta bantu ekyo okwenywereza mu bufuzi.  
Ate essira liyinza okuteekebwa ku nkola erina okugobererwa abantu bonna era kino ne kikozesebwa okulaga obuzibu Rwanda bw'eyolekaganye nabwo mu by'obufuzi obwesigamiziddwa ku njawukana mu mawanga.
Bannabyabufuzi mu mawanga g'Abazungu basobola okulwanirira ensonga ezikwata ku bantu gamba ng'ensonga ekwata ku by'obulamu.
Abafirika bo balwanirira kumanyika.
Nga kampeyini yaabwe bagyesigamizizza ku nsonga ezikwata ku bantu bonna, ekibiina kya Social Democratic Party kiringa ekisaagirira obusaagirizi.
Mu ngeri endala, bawagizi ba Kagame.
Kati nkitegeera bulungi nti Abanyarwanda si bantu bazibu nnyo.
