Okuvumirira gavumenti kiwa ebbeetu abo abeesimbyewo okumenya amateeka?
Ebimu ku ebyo bye batuuseeko bizingiramu bino wammanga:
Gavumenti ekoze nnyo mu by'enjigiriza.
Amasomero g'obuyigirize obwa waggulu geeyongedde obungi okuva ku limu okutuuka ku makumi abiri.
Ng'ekyokulabirako, ebintu ebyetaagisibwa mu bulamu obwa bulijjo.
Bye bakola birina okulabikira ku mikuttu gy'eby'empuliziganya.
Yagamba nti amaggye g'alina si matendeke bulungi.
Amaggye gatandise okulya ssente.
Abakulu mu bitundu n'abakungu mu disitulikiti baategezebwa.
Kino kyakolebwa oluvannyuma lw'okubuuza amayitire g'abaduumizi.
Kusoomooza ki kw'oyolekaganye nakwo?
Okumu ku kusoomooza kwe twolekaganya nakwo kwe kufuna ebikozesebwa mu kusoggola omwenge.
Gavumenti ekoze enteekateeka ennaasobozesa buli muntu okuba ne yinsuwa y'obulamu.
Ng'eyambibwako ab'emikwano mu nsi ez'ebweru.
Tasobola kubeera wamu n'abantu abalala olw'emisango gye yazza mu kitundu.
Olw'okukimanya nti bajja kuyigganyizibwa era nga tekijja kubabeerera kyangu kubeera wamu n'abantu abalala.
Olunaku lwo olutandika otya?
Okweyongerayongera kw'abantu kinnakola ki ku bungi bw'emmere?
Okweyongerayongera mu bungi bw'abantu kuli ebitundu 3.2 ku buli kikumi bw'ogeraageranya n'okweyongerayongera kw'obungi bw'abantu mu nsi yonna okuli ekitundu 1.2 ku buli kikumi.
Ng'ekyokulabirako, okubeera n'abalimi abatendekeddwa obulungi era nga baagala kye bakola kijja kuba kya muganyulo nnyo mu by'obulimi.
Era bwe kityo bwe kirina okuba ne ku bitongole ebirala mu by'enfuna by'eggwanga.
Embeera y'obudde ekyukakyuka kusoomooza kwa maanyi nnyo eri busineesi.
Abantu mu nsi yonna balina okuba n'ebyetaagisa nga mu bino mwe muli obuttimba bw'ensiri, eddagala erifuuyiri ebiwuka mu mayumba n'eddagala eddungi erikozesebwa mu bulamu.
Eddagala lya tetenasi, ely'ekiziyiiro, ery'okukolola, ery'endwadde z'ekibumba, poliyo ne lukusense.
Eddagala erigema omusujja gw'ensiri liyinza okukozesebwa awamu n'enteekateeka eriwo mu kiseera kino ey'okujjanjjabamu omusujja gw'ensiri awamu n'okugema.
Era wajja kubaawo enteekateeka ekolebwa awantu wonna mu nsi okusobozesa abakugu okunoonyereza ku ddagala ly'omusujja gw'ensiri.
Wabeewo enteekateeka ekolebwa okulwanyisa omusujja gw'ensiri obutaddamu kubaawo.
Swiiti ng'aweza obukadde abiri mu bubiri n'ekitundu, ebizigo ebiweza obukadde kkumi, ennyama y'omu bikebe eweza obukadde buna mu emitwalo kyenda n'ebiriisa ebirala ebiweza obukadde mukaaga mu emitwalo attaano.
Bikozesebwa mu kwoza amakyuppa agaba gakozeeko agateekebwamu eby'okunywa mu makolero.
Kino kikolebwa nnyo mu makolero amatonotono mangi agali mu maka g'abantu kinnoomu.
Tewaliiwo ngeri yonna gy'oyinza kugenda mu maka g'omuntu okulaba obanga mulimu ekkolero.
Bino bizingiramu amata g'obuwunga, eby'okunywa, eddagala ly'amannyo, ssabuuni, buto, ebizigo, sirapu n'emyenge.
Kino kiri bwe kityo olw'amateeka g'eby'obusuubuzi amanafu n'abo abeeyita abasigansimbi abeeyongedde obungi.
Yanenya abasigansimbi ab'ebikyupuli olw'okukola ebintu ebitatuukana na mutindo n'okukopperera eby'abalala.
Obuli bw'enguzi bulina okukolebwako n'amaanyi mangi ate mu bwangu ddala.
Kino kirina okukolebwa okuyitira mu kusomesa abantu baffe ebikwata ku kufuna tenda, okuwagira engeri ennungi ey'okugulamu ebintu, n'okuba n'amazima mu by'emisolo era ne mu ngeri y'okuddukanyaamu emirimu.
Nga tetunnatunuulira kitundu kyaffe, essira tusaanidde okulissa ku kufuna abantu abalina obukugu okusobola okuleetawo enkulaakulana mu nsi yoffe.
Okufaananako abo abakola mu malongosezzo g'emmottoka, abavubuka abaweereza bamakanika, abo abakola mu ssaaluuni, n'abaweesi.
Ensi yaffe esigadde njavu ekiviiriddeko eby'obulimu obutaba birungi.
Mukole ku kizibu ekikwata ku tteeka ly'ettaka abantu basobole okuba n'obwannanyini ku ttaka.
Okuviira ddala ku bikozesebwa ebituufu, enkola ennungi, omutindo omulungi n'akatale.
Enkulaakulana etuukagana obulungi n'ensi yaffe.
Baawagira eky'abantu aba bulijjo bannakigwanyizi okujja mu buyinza ate nga tebalina busobozi bwa kutereeza nsi.
Si kituufu kugamba nti demokulasiya aleeta demokulasiya.
Amaggye amagwiira gaalina ekigendererwa eky'okukuumira emmabega enkyukakyuka ezandireeteddwa eggye ery'amaanyi eryandisobodde okuzzaawo emirembe mu
Embeera eyaliwo yali yeetaagisa eggye ennafu era nga teririna bumanyirivu.
Ekintu kyonna nga si kufa, tekiyinza kulemesa muntu kubaako ky'akola.
Kyakola enteekateeka okusinziira ku ndowooza y'ekisiraamu ey'obumu era ne kitandika okussa mu nkola amateeka ga Sharia.
Nneewunya nnyo amagezi ge yalina ku nsonga eno.
Yagamba nti abagwiira boonoona eby'obufuzi bw'ensi nga bassaawo abawanguzi n'abawangulibwa.
Okufuna obuyambi okuva eri abagwiira kireetera abawanguzi okulemererwa okukozesa eby'obufuzi eby'omunda okugatta abantu ne basalawo okwesigama ku bagwiira.
Demokulasiya abaawo mu nsi omuli obutebenkevu so si omuli entalo.
Kyokka okusoomoozebwa okwaliwo kwali kwekuusa ku ngeri y'okutegeezaamu abantu nga tobaleetedde kukuba miranga.
Monday akulira okulwanyisa ebikolwa by'ekitujju
Kyokka, ekiwandiiko kyagamba nti ng'Abasiraamu, abavubuka tebaali basanyufu.
Kino tekisaanidde kubuusibwamu maaso oba okutwalibwa ng'ekikulu kubanga bano abavubuka Basiraamu abasaba entakera emirundi ettaano buli lunaku.
Tebaateebwa okutuusa nga wayiseewo emyaka ena.
Ebisuubizo bino ebitaatuukirizibwa byayongera okuleeta obutali bumativu.
Baali bamanyi enteekateeka zaabwe ez'omunda, enkola yaabwe, amannya, gye bava, ne nnamba z'emmottoka ez'ab'eby'okwerinda.
N'olwekyo ekizibu tekyali nti bali tebamanyi kya kukola wabula engeri y'okukikolamu.
Bino byonna byesigamizibwa ku ebyo ebyazuulibwa ku mitwe ebiri egyabetentebwa ejja abasajja abasuubirwa okuba nga be baatulisa bbomu mu bifo ebyo byombi.
Abantu abo ababiri abatulisa bbomu tebannamanyika.
Abalwanyi bano batandika okwezza ebitundu ebimu mu ggwanga gye baali bayinza okubaako kye bafuna.
Ayisibwamu amaaso olw'okulemera mu buyinza ng'akulembera gavumenti embi.
Baali ba mu kibiina ky'Abasiraamu ekya Salaf ne Tablique.
Nga bakolera ab'eby'okwerinda, okweyongera mu maaso n'obulumbaganyi bwabwe nga batulisa bbomu mu bantu era n'okweyongera okuyingizaamu abantu ng'essira okusingira ddala balissizza ku bantu abayigirize awatali kufaayo ku ddiini.
Nga balowooza nti bandifunye okusonyiyibwa, okusasulwa ssente oba okufuna emirimu mu maggye ne mu bitongole ebirala eby'okwerinda.
Bbomu ze beetulisizzaamu zitera kusanyaawo omubiri gwonna naye omutwe n'emikono ne bisigalawo.
Mu Korani mwalimu ennamba z'essimu ezaayamba ennyo poliisi okumanya ebikulu.
Bbomu yali egaanye okubwattuka ku lunaku olwali luyise.
Okusinziira ku bino, ab'eby'okwerinda baatandika okugoberera ennamba z'essimu endala ezaali zikubiddwako nga Jjulaayi 11 nga bakozesa essimu eyo.
Kino kiraga nti ab'eby'okwerinda balina ebituufu bye bamanyi ebisobola okubayamba okulondoola abatujju.
Tewaliiwo kirala kyakolebwa.
Abatujju beewala ebifo awali obukuumi obw'amaanyi ne bagenda gye batusuubirwa.
Ensonda endala zigamba nti abatujju baasobola okukola ekyo olw'obuli bw'enguzi obuli mu kitongole ky'eby'okwerinda ekyaviirako okulekera awo okukola okunoonyereza.
Ssente eziteekebwa mu kitongole ky'eby'okwerinda zikozesebwa abakulu okweggagawaza kino ne kireetera abalina okukola omulimu okuba nga tebalina ssente za kukozesa.
Eby'okwerinda by'eggwanga byonooneddwa olw'okwagala okweggagawaza.
Abo abalina okukola emirimu beemulugunya olw'okuba tebasobola kutuukiriza mirimu gyabwe.
Yassaawo enkola esobozesa buli aba akoze omulimu okufuna omuganyulo.
Eby'obukeesi ebisinga obungi tebyali byangu era kino kyaleetera ebikolwa by'abatujju okweyongera obungi.
Ebitongole ebikeesi byayingirira enteekateeka z'eby'empuliziganya, ensimbi ezikozesebwa era ne bitabulatabula ebibinja by'abatujju.
Abantu baakwatibwa, baatulugunyizibwa era okuteebwa kwabwe kwesigamizibwa ku ssente.
Yali avumirira nnyo eky'okusiba abantu nga tebamaze kuwozesebwa era n'eky'okubatulugunya.
Yakiggumizza nti ajja kukola ku muntu yenna atulugunya abalala.
Abo abateeberezebwa nti beenyigira mu bikolwa eby'ekitujju balina okunoonyerezebwako ekimala ate oluvannyuma bakwasibwe poliisi.
N'olwekyo, ssente ezeetaagisibwa okukola omulimu tezaayongezebwako.
Emirimu ming gyayimirira era n'egyali gikoleddwako emmabega tegyeyongera mu maaso.
Ebitongole by'okwerinda biremeseddwa olw'okubulwa ssente.
Ssente ezaali ziweereddwa ebitongole by'okwerinda zaabulankanyizibwa abakulu.
Bakyewaggula beefuula okuba abatunda ebintu nga babitambuza, ababodaboda, era ng'abavuzi ba takisi.
Abazannyi b'omupiira baakubirizibwa okwewala ebikolwa by'okwegatta awamu n'ebikolwa ebirala ebitali birungi mu kiseera eky'okuzannya omupiira.
Kino kyali kityo olw'obutali bulambulukufu obwali mu bitongole by'okwerinda.
Ebibiina by'abayeekera ebyali bisanyiziddwawo byasikirwa ebirala.
Abayeekera kati basazeewo okukozesa abakazi mu kifo ky'okukozesa abasajja basobole okumalawo okwekengerwa.
Ow'eby'okwerinda yaggyibwawo.
Okwongera okutulisa bbomu mu bantu nnaddala mu bifo omuli abantu abangi ennyo.
Mweyongere okuwandiisa abantu ng'essira mulissa ku abo abayigirize awatali kufaayo ku ddiini.
kyokka beeyongera okulimba.
Ebiwandiiko bino bibasobozesa okuva mu kifo ekimu okudda mu kirala, era kireetera abantu obutasobola kubeekengera okuba abantu ababi.
Okusengukasenguka kukendedde.
Kino kikoleddwa okulemesa ab'eby'okwerinda okukola okunoonyereza.
Abantu abamu balowooza nti gavumenti ekozesa omulimu gwaffe okunyigiriza bannabyabufuzi oba abo be balowooza nti balabe ba gavumenti.
Enkola eyeesigamiziddwa ku mateeka eyatandikibwawo kampuni z'amasimu nga zaagala kkooti okufuna lisiiti okusobola okubaako bye basasula, si nnungi era eviirako okulwa. 
Bizibu okulabirira.
Obuzibu obwo bulina okubaawo
Kiba kyetaagisa okuba omuvumu era omwegendereza nga buli muntu yeekuuma.
Okuva bwe kituuka n'ebunaayira, kiba kitegeeza nti balina okukolera awamu.
Bwe baatandika okukola amafuta aga ethanol, waliwo ebirala ebitali birungi ebyavaamu ate nga tebyasuubirwa.
Okusinziira ku ebyo ebibaawo mu bulamu obwa bulijjo, okwefuga ebintu kiviiriddeko enkola ey'obufuzi bw'amatwale obw'ekiseera kino era nga ensi nnyingi enkuseere ziraga obuwulize olw'obwetaavu bwe zirina.
Ebibiina by'abalwanyi Abasiraamu bimalirivu okubunyisa enkola yaabwe mu buli kanyomero k'ensi.
Ekitundu eky'okusatu kijja kufulumira mu kitundu ekiddako.
Ebyo ebyayogerwa ku kiwandiiko ky'Abanyarwanda bireetera abantu okuleekera awo okuteebereza ku ekyo ky'alowooza.
Tebasaanidde kwewunya olw'enneeyisa eyo eyoleka obukambwe.
Abo abamumanyi bamanyi bulungi engeri gy'alemera ku ndowooza ye k'ebe ntuufu oba nkyamu.
Wadde nga kiri bwe kityo, waliwo ensonga z'ayogerako ezirina okulowoozebwako ennyo.
Wadde nga tekiri mu mbeera nnungi, kiyinza obuteetaagisa kwogerwako mu ngeri egudde olubege.
Teryalina bakozi, poliisi, malwaliro era oboolyawo n'ekisinga obubi ennyingiza mu by'ensimbi.
Okumala emyaka, abagabirizi b'obuyambi babadde balowooza nti gavumenti empya tejja kuwangaala olw'okusalibwako obuyambi.
Bannaabwe abaawanduka mu lwokaano kati bakolera wamu n'ab'eby'okwerinda.
Abantu abalala bonna balowooza nti bayigganyizibwa lwa ddiini.
Enkuba ntono era n'enzizzi zitandise okukalira era n'aw'okulimira tewakyamala.
Emiwendo gyalinnya olw'okuba abalimi baalekera awo okulima kasooli ow'emmere n'ow'okuliisa ebisolo ne batandika okulima ow'okukolamu amafuta.
Abantu bukadde na bukadde abali mu nsi ezikyakula baali mu kabi okukudda mu bunkuseere, era bano basaasaanya ssente ze bafuna ebitundu nkaaga mu bitaano ku buli kikumi mu kuguala eby'okulya. 
Kino kijja kulinyisa nnyo emiwendo gy'eby'entambula kiviireko n'eby'amaguzi ng'amafuta okulinnya ebbeeyi.
Mu bwangu ddala, buli kanyomero konna ak'ensi kalina okutwala eby'ekijaasi okuba ekintu ekikulu ennyo era n'okwerinda ebikolwa eby'ekitujju.
Baabikozesa okuliisa abantu abo bennyini abeenyigira mu kittabantu.
Bwe tutabaako kye tukolawo, ffenna tujja kukosebwa.
Era tulina okutandika okulowooza ku birala eby'okukozesa nga mw'otwalidde okugema omusujja gw'ensiri, era kino kiyinza okuyambako enkola eriwo mu kiseera kino.
Okugema kuyambye nnyo mu kutereeza obulamu bw'abantu mu Afirica okumala emyaka mingi egiyise.
Tuli batono nnyo abatannakwatibwa bulwadde obwo naye omuntu yenna alina omwana eyali akwatiddwa omusujja gw'ensiri amanyi nga bwe kiri ekikulu okufuna eddagala erigema omusujja gw'ensiri.
Emyaka mingi egiyise we nnatandikira okukola ng'omusawo agaba eddagala, kyali tekirowoozeka nti eddagala erigema omusujja gw'ensiri lisobola okufunika.
Tunaatera okufuna eddagala eryo.
Abo abakola amateeka kijja kubeetaagisa okussaawo enkola enneegobererwa era ennenyweza eby'obulamu.
Kino kiba kizingiramu byonna okuviira ddala ku kutereeza enkola egobererwa, enkola ey'okubitambuza, n'okutendeka abasawo okusobola okugema.
Bino biyinza okwongerezebwa ku ebyo ebiriwo mu kiseera kino okusobola okufuna ebikozesebwa ebirala, gamba nga eddagala erigema eriyitibwa rotavirus ne pneumococcal.
N'abantu abalala balina okwenyigiramu.
Ebiragalalagala ebikozesebwa bigulibwa okusingira ddala amakolero amatono agakola eby'okunywa.
Kino kisobola okubeera eky'akabi eri obulamu bw'abo ababikozesa.
Awa okulabula ku bimu ku bintu ebyo bye balina ku lukalala ebiyinza okuba nga byayitako.
Twetaaga ssente ezimala okusobola okunyikizza okuyigiriza kwaffe eri abantu nga tubalabula.
Twagala poliisi ebowe ebintu ebiteeberezebwa okuba nga byayitako era batuyite.
Twagala kituuke ku ssa eryo nga tekikoma bukomi ku kukwata bantu olw'okuzza emisango kubanga kiri mu mateeka agafuga Poliisi.
Yagamba nti olw'amateeka amanafu, abantu bwe bakwatibwa basasula ssente ne beddirayo okukola emirimu gyabwe."
Amateeka amakakali gayinza okuyambako.
Ebyo ebiva mu buli bw'enguzi bikosa bonna.
Nze ndowooza nti ebintu bibiri ku ebyo ebisinga obukulu ebiyinza okuyamba mu kulwanyisa obuli bw'enguzi kwe kuyamba abantu okuba n'empisa ennungi.
Abasuubuzi bangi mu Uganda balina ekizibu eky'obutaba na kumanya, bayinza batya okuyambibwa?
Tulina enkola ey'eby'empuliziganya gye tukola enneetusobozesa okumanya ebibafaako nabo okumanya ebitukwatako.
Okufuba kwaffe kujja kusobozesa abalala abakola busineesi okufuna okumanya okwetaagisa.
Abantu abakola obulungi emirimu bamugaso nnyo eri enkulaakulana y'ensi.
Ensonga eno ekwata ku bakozi abalina obukugu si ya kakati era kino kirina okutereezebwa okuyitira mu nkola ennuŋŋamu.
Enkola eno ejja kubaleetera okuba nga tebeetya era ejja kubasobozesa okwenyigira mu mirimu gyonna eginnabaawo.
Kino kituukidde mu kiseera ng'eggwanga lyeyongeddemu abantu olw'okuba bazaala nnyo.
Emmere bw'eba nga ntono ku bantu abali mu ggwanga, awo ab'olina ekizibu kya maanyi.
Wadde ng'obungi bw'abantu abankuseere mu Uganda bukendeddeko gyebuvuddeko awo, abantu obukadde nga buna, nga kimu kyakubiri ku bo batwalibwa okuba abo abakolerera okubaawo obubeezi. 
Kijja kusoboka okukola eby'obulimi ku kigero ekinene n'ekitono singa ffenna ng'eggwanga era ng'abantu kinnoomu twongera ssente mu by'obulimi.
Era tulina okuteeka ssente mu kudaabiriza ebintu nga mw'otwalidde n'embeera etwetoolodde.
Sebaggala yagaana okukkiriza nti yasala eddiiro n'adda mu kibiina kya National Resistance Movement emyaka ena emabega
Naye kikyamu ki ekiri mu kukolagana ne Museveni n'ekibiina kya NRM?
Baali baagala mbeerenga Ssebaana eyamala ebiseera bye byonna ng'awanyisaganya ebigambo ne Museveni?
Sebaggala yeesimbawo okulondebwa nga pulezidenti w'Ekibiina kya DP mu ttabamiruka w'ekibiina e Mbale mu Febwali omwaka guno naye Norbert Mao n'amuwangula
Bannakibiina abaaliwo mu lukuŋŋana e Mbale bagamba nti sente Sebaggala ze yagaba ng'olukuŋŋaana terunatandika era nga lugenda mu maaso, zeewuunyisa nnyo abantu wa gye yazigya
Bagamba nti bwe yasisinkananga bamemba b'Ekibiina kya DP, Sebaggala yayogeranga ku ky'okugabana obuyinza ne Museveni
Kyewuunyisa okuba nti yali ayogera ku kukola bizineensi ne Museveni singa alemwa okufuna ebitundu ataano ku kikumi mu kulonda okujja
Abamu bangamba nti Sebaggala yawa abamu ku bagenyi emifaliso
Beewuunya engeri UPDF gye yawaayo emifaliso gyayo okuvujjirira olukuŋŋaana lw'abo bali ku ludda oluvuganya okugyako nga waliwo omukungu okuva mu gavumenti awagira Sebaggala okufuuka pulezidenti w'Ekibiina kya DP
Kino kyawaliriza abalaba ebigenda mu maaso okugamba nti Sebaggala amaze ekiseera ng'akola entegeka okuwaayo ekibiina kya DP eri Museveni ne NRM, naye ekigenderwa kye kyagwa butaka mu lukuŋŋaana olwali e Mbale
NRM yasanyukira okujja kwa Sebaggala
Omwogezi w'ekibiina kya NRM, Mary Karooro Okurut yawandiika nti: "Sebaggala y'omu ku bantu abatono mu Uganda asukkulumako kato ku bantu kinnoomu
Mabikke yasambajja ekya Sebaggala okuba omututumufu
Mabikke yagamba nti omuddo gumaze okukitta
Mabikke agamba nti ekibiina kya NRM kyerimbalimba nti Sebaggala ky'ekyokulwanyisa kye bajja okukozesa okusaanyaawo oludda oluvuganya n'okuddamu okuwamba Kampala
Eyesimbawo ku ludda oluvuganya ow'ekibiina kya FDC Dr Kizza Besigye yafuna obululu 245,004 nga bino bye bitundu ataano ku buli kikumu ku bululu bwonna obwakubibwa
Eyesimbawo mu Kibiina kya DP Ssebaana Kizito yafuna obululu 11,993, Abed Bwanika 3,045 Miria Obote 1,425
Museveni yafuna obululu 170,688 
Singa ebyava mu kulonda mu 2006 bye bikozesebwa, Sebaggala tayinza kuwaayo Kampala eri ekibiina kya NRM
Mu kibiina kya Progressive Democratic Party yamalamu bbanga ki?
Mabikke agamba nti Basentebe bonna mu Kampala okugyako Godfrey Nyakana era n'ababaka ba palimenti bonna okugyako Freddie Ruhindi, baali basaale mu kunoonyezza Sebaggala akalulu mu 2006, naye okuva olwo, tebakolagana naye
Akiriziganya n'ekigambibwa nti Sebaggala tayinza kuwangula okulonda ku lulwe yekka
Omukugu mu kunoonyereza okuva e Makerere Institute of Social Research, Golooba Mutebi, naye akkiriza nti Sebaggala talina kintu kyonna kya byabufunzi ekiyinza okuyamba NRM

Giddudu omusango yagugoba mu Maayi
Lubega yasaba kooti okugyawo olukungaana olwaliwo mu Febwari mu Mbale olw'abakungu abaalonda Mao ng'omukulembeze w'Ekibiina kya Demokulase

Naye omulamuzi yagoba omusango, Lubega ne banne mwe baali beetwala okuba abakulembeze b'Ekibiina kya Demokulase
Mbidde yagamba oyo eyesimbawo awatali kibiina nti ekiwandiiko kya kooti akitute eri Akakiiko k'Eby'Okulonda era nti poliisi ekwate Lubega ne banne singa beeyongera okwelaga mu lujjudde bakulembeze b'ekibiina kya DP
Lubega yagamba nti talabangako kiwandiiko kuva mu kooti era nti ne balooyabe tebakifunangako
Yagamba nti Mbidde yali alimba
Yagamba nti Mbidde yali teyeerabidde kiragiro kya kooti ekigamba nti yali ajjulira
Lubega yagamba nti nga Okutoba 7, yajulira eky'okugoba omusango gwe era nti omusango gwali gulinda kuwulirwa
Yabyogera wadde nga kooti yali egobye omusango gwe, teyalangirira obanga obukulembeze bwa Mao mu Kibiina kya Demokulase bwali bukkirizibwa mu mateeka
Mbidde yagamba nti tebaafuna kiragiro kya kooti kyonna ekikwata ku kujulira kwa Lubega
Yagamba nti okusalawo okwo kwaganyula bo era okujulira kwa Lubega kwalina akakwate nakwo
Mbidde yagamba nti "okujulira kujja kuwulirwa emyaka ebiri okuva kati"
Kyokka Mbidde agamba nti ekiragiro kya kooti yakitwala ku poliisi n'eri Kakiiko k'Eby'Okulonda, naye omwogezi wa poliisi mu Bendobendo lya Kampala Idi Senkumba yagamba nti yali takirabangako

Okusiinziira ku Golooba Mutebi, akabi akali mu biwandiiko ngebyo y'engeri gye bireetawo endowooza ku Afirika etali ntuufu wadde nga biwa ekifaananyi kinene ku ekyo abantu kye bamanyi
Golooba Mutebi agamba nti, batera okukitwala nti ensi z'Afirika tezikulaakulana era endowooza ezo zikomyawo ekifaananyi ekyo
Mutebi agamba nti,okukkiriza ebintu ebitawa kifaananyi kituufu ku ngeri ensi z'Afirika gye zikolamu, kyeyoleka kaati, era kikontana n'endowooza ezo
Mutebi akiraba nti akakiiko okugaana okugaba ekirabo okutuusa ng'emitendera gigobereddwa, kiyamba okukendeeza ku kufuula ekirabo obutaba ky'amakulu.

Ani yawa ekiragiro okufulumya ebivuddemu? Yagamba nti yali Kadaga
Agamba Kadaga teyandiwagidde Moses Kizige avuvuganya ne Menhya e Bugabula w'e Bukiika kkono, yavuganya Kibalya mu Bukiika ddyo wa Bugabula ne Martin Muzaale n'avuganya Isaac
Abo bonna abaawagirwa Kadaga baawangula akalulu ak'okususula
Gavumenti n'omukungu w'ekibiina kya NRM, Daudi Migereko babuusabuusa emisango gye baateeka ku Kadaga
Agamba nti kya bulijjo abapya okutuukirira abakulembeze abateekebwawo nga Kadaga ku bikwata ku biruubirwa byabwe
Eyali Ssentebbe wa Disitulikiti ya Iganga Patrick Bageya agamba nti obukuubagano bubaddengawo mu bufuzi bwa Busoga okuva mu mu 1986

Akakuubangano wakati wa Kadaga ne Kivejinja kaasigala wadde nga Kazibwe yava mu lukiiko lwa baminisita

Bageya agamba nti Katuntu yaletebwa Kadaga era n'alagirwa Kazibwe okuwangula Kivejinja
Abasajja basatu basobola batya okuganga nti omukazi omu yabalemesa?
Agamba Kiyingi yawangulwa olw'okuba yagaana okuwagira omulangira William Gabula eyasaba entebe ya Kyabazinga
Omusango gwa Kiyingi gwe gumu ku misango egigenda okutunulwamu akakiiko akaawamu akatondebwawo ekibiina kya NRM  okwekenneenya n'okuganjoola enkayana z'eby'okulonda, naye akakiiko kaali tekannatuuza lukiiko lwonna
Wadde ng'akakiiko kaagenda e Kamuli, kaali kasobola okuemesa Kadaga memba w'akakiiko Akafuzi ak'ekibiina era  Omumyuka w'Omwogezi wa palamenti?
Mu mwaka gwa 2008, bannabya bufuzi era tebakkiriziganya ku ngeri Kiyingi gye yakwatamu omusango gwa Kadaga gwe yawaaba mu kakiiko ka palamenti ogukwata ku mateeka, enkizo n'empisa, nga bavunaana omubaka wa palamenti ow'e Kibuku Saleh Kamba okwonoona erinnya ly'abala  
Mu lukungana lw'akabondo k'ababaka ba NRM, Kamba yanenya Kadaga olw'okuwagira katuntu n'awangula Kiveijinja mu kulonda okwaddibwamu mu Novemba 2007 okw'ekifo ky'omubaka wa palamenti e Bugwere

Wiiki ewedde, Kudeeba yagamba ab'olupapula lwa Independent nti ekibiina kyali kisazeewo okugenda mu maaso n'ebyava mu  kulonda ebyasooka ebyawanguza Nagudi

Abakulembeze abamu mu kibiina bawa endowooza zaabwe mu mawulire naye Besigye teyawa ndowooza ye wabula yalinda akalulu kasalewo eggoye
Abbey Semuwemba munnayuganda abeera mu Bungereza
Omuntu yenna bwaba ayagala okuyingira palamenti, addukire mu state house afune emikisa gya pulezidenti Museveni oba amufukeko amafuta 
Okulonda kw'ekibiina kya NRM kubaddemu obukambwe n'obulimba obufuuse obw'olulango kumpi mu nsi yonna
Kino kyavaamu bannabyabufuzi ba NRM  bangi okunyiikaala era ne bagamba nti baagala kwesimbawo ku bwannamunigina
Pulesidenti Musevini yali asazeewo okubatwala nga bakyewaggula era n'atiisatiisa okubagoba mu kibiina kya NRM.
Naye oluvannyuma lw'okusisinkana bamemba b'ekibiina ab'akabondo ka palamenti, yakyusa endowooza ye n'asalawo abaleke beesimbewo bwannamunigina nga tebalina kibiina mwebajjidde.
Olw'okuba baali bangi nnyo abaali batayiseemu ku kusunsulibwa kw'ekibiina kya NRM, pulezidenti kye yakola kyali kya magezi nnyo.
Museveni ayinza okuba nga yatya nti singa abagaana okwesimbawo ku lwabwe, bayinza okusala eddiiro ne badda ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti.
N'olwekyo, kirabika tujja kuba n'abo abeesimbyewo ku lwabwe kumpi mu buli disitulikiti.
Era kisoboka okuba nti abannesimbawo ku lwabwe abasinga obungi bajja kuba ba mu kibiina kya NRM.
Kino kiba kitegeeza nti NRM eyinza okuba n'abeesimbyewo mu konsituwensi abawera ababiri.
Olw'okuba oludda oluvuganya gavumenti terusobola kusimbawo babaka mu konsituwensi zonna, kirabika aba NRM bajja kuba bavuganya na ba NRM bannaabwe.
Kino kiba kitegeeza nti NRM ne bwetandikkiriza byabufuzi eby'ebibiina ebingi, obukuubagano obuli munda mu kyo mwenyini  bwenditaddewo embeera eringa ey'ebibiina ebingi.
Eky'ab'oludda oluvuganya gavumenti okulemererwa okusikiriza aba NRM abatali bamativu tekyesigamye ku kuba nti tebalina birowoozo birungi.
Tukimanyi bulungi nti abasinga obungi ku abo abali mu NRM nabo balina endowoozo ng'eya abo abali ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti ku bikwata ku buli bw'enguzi, ku butaba na bumanyirivu ne ku ngeri etali nnungi eggwanga lino gye likulembeddwamu.
Naye ekitulemye okutegeera ye ngeri NRM gy'erina abawagizi abangi
Museveni akoze kyonna ekisoboka okukakasa nti wabaawo enkola eyeefanaanyiriza enfuga ya demokulasiya.
olw'okuba akkirizza okulonda okubaawo mu kibiina entakera, bangi abawadde akakisa okulinya amadaala g'obukulembeze mu kibiina kya NRM.
Museveni akimanyi bulungi nnyo nti okulonda kiba kiseera kya kugezesa obuganzi munnabyabufuzi bw'aba alina mu bantu.
Naye era ayagala NRM ewangulire waggulu esobole okuba ng'esukuluma ku bibiina ebirala.
Kino kikulu nnyo okulemesa abali mu kibiina okukivaamu ne bayingira mu bibiina ebiri ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti.
Ng'ekyokulabirako, NRM ekiraze nti teyinza kuwangulibwa mu Buggwanjuba bwa Uganda.
N'olwekyo, oli ne bw'abanga ng'avumirira nnyo NRM eyo ku ludda olw'Ebuggwanjuba, tayinza kudda ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti.
Ng'ekyokulabirako, lowooza ku Alex Ruhunda eyalondebwa gyebuvuddeko awo okukwatira NRM bendera mu Fort Portal.
Nnagamba nti NRM esaanidde okusiimibwa olw'okutumbula n'okuleetawo enkyukakyuka mu by'enfuna mu myaka kkumi egiyise.
Ruhunda yannyigira nnyo olw'okubaako ekintu ekirungi kye njogera ku NRM.
Yagamba nti Museveni yangulirira.
Abantu bangi bayinza okugamba nti ekyo Ruhunda kye yakola tekirina we kikwataganira n'engeri ye ng'omuntu, n'empisa ze era n'obwesigwa bwe.
Naye bw'aba ow'okugenda mu palamenti, ateekeddwa okubeera mu kibiina kya NRM era awo ab'ajja kubeera mu kabondo akakola obulungi munda mu kibiina okusobola okuleetawo enkyukakyuka.
Endowooza y'obutawangulwa Museven n'ekibiina kya NRM ebadde egobererwa okumala emyaka mingi, y'eviiriddeko bannabyabufuzi bangi okwesimbawo ku lwabwe
Era eyo ye nsonga lwaki abo aboogerera ennyo NRM basalawo ne bayingira ekibiina ekyo.
Museveni awa empeera oyo yenna akkiriza obukulembeze bwe wadde ng'akimanyidde ddala nti tebakkiriziganya na byabufuzi bwe.
Museveni akimanyi nti okulondamu abagezi kyangu okusinga okubalwanyisa.
Oluusi kino akikozesa okusobola okunyigiriza abo ababa basazeewo okumusoomooza nga bwe kiri ku Besigye
Ng'ayitira mu kuwa empeera abo abeesigwa gyali, era n'akaluubiriza nnyo abo abali ku ludda oluvuganya gavumenti, pulezidenti atiisizza nnyo abo abandyagadde okuva mu NRM era n'abo abandyagadde okulwanyisa obufuzi bwe.
Eky'okuba nti Museveni mwetegefu okwaniriza bannabyabufuzi ababadde bamuwakanya, kituukaganye n'abamu kye bayita "okusalawo okw'obulimba."  Abantu beefuula okuba abawagira NRM wadde nga ekituufu kiri nti tebagiwagira.
Bannabyabufuzi mu Uganda boolekaganye n'okusalawo okweyongera okuba abawulize eri Museveni ne beeyongera okuba n'obuyinza era n'enkizo oba okumuwakanya ne bafuna ebizibu nga Besigye.
Ebigambo ebisembayo bikulu nnyo era biraga ensonga lwaki abo ababa tebayiseemu tabayinza kwesoga mu FDC, Museveni akimanyi nti ekiseera eky'okulonda kigezesa obuganzi munnabyabufuzi bw'aba alina mu bantu.
Pulesidenti Museveni yasisinkana abawagizi b'ekibiina kye abawera nga enkumi satu abaava e Mawokota North constituency, mu disitulikiti y'e Mpigi.
Omumbejja w'ekitundu ekyo Amelia Kyambadde ate nga yaliko omuwandiisi ow'ekyama owa pulezidenti, ye yategeka olukuŋŋaana olwo
Ekigendererwa ky'olukuŋŋaana olwo kwali okumatiza omubaka wa palamenti ow'ekitundu ekyo Claver Mutuluuza obuteesimba ku Amelia Kyambadde mu kulonda okuddako.
Kyambadde ajja kuba mwangu mu kulonda kw'ababaka ba palaminti mu 2011 ne bw'anaaba ng'awagiddwa Museveni.
Okusinziira ku bigambo ebyava mu State House, Mutuluuza yagamba pulezidenti nti yakigenderera okwesimbawo ku lulwe "olwa demokulasiya n'ebbettu erimuweebwa mu ssemateeka." 
Njakuba n'ekifaananyi kya Mutuluuza era n'ekya pulezidenti kubanga ndi muwagizi we.
Museveni simulinako kizibu kyonna.
Njagala kwebaza Amelia olw'enkulaakulana gy'aleese e Mawokota North
Singa nnaweebwa ssente nnange nnandikoze ekintu kye kimu
Yagamba nti "abantu abamu mu Muvumenti baasiiwuka empisa."
Ba Muvumenti mu bigambo mwokka naye si mu bikolwa," bw'atyo Museveni bwe yayogera ng'ajuliriza ku bigambo bya Mutuluuza.
Museveni yamusuubiza okumuwa obwa minisita singa teyeesimbawo mu 2011.
Ekyo tekyali kya bulijjo era kirabika kyakanga nnyo Museveni.
Enjawukana ebaddewo wakati wa Mutuluuza ne Amelia si ye yokka ebaddewo mu kibiina kya NRM mu kulonda okw'okusunsulibwamu okubadde kwakabaawo mu ggwanga lyonna.
Emisango egisukka mu lukaaga egyekuusa ku bubbi bw'obululu gyawaabirwa eri akakiiko ka NRM ak'eby'okulonda era abo abaagwa batiitiisa okunaabira pulezidenti Museven mu maaso
Museven akimanyi nti batono nnyo ku abo abandigaanye okulondebwa okuba baminisita oba okuweebwa omulimu omulala gwonna mu gavumenti.
Take Agaba Abbas eyaliko omukulembeze w'abavubuka mu NRM eyawangulibwa mu kalulu k'abo abanaakwatira ekibiina bbendera mu Kitagwenda, mu disitulikiti y'e Kamwenge
Yawaaba omusango ogwekuusa ku by'okulonda ng'agamba nti omubaka wa NRM aliko era nga y'akwatidde NRM bbendera, Nulu Byamukama yatiisatiisa nnyo abalonzi era yakozesa ebikolwa eby'obukambwe bingi ekyaviirako abamu ku bawagizi be okufumitibwa ebiso.
Kyokka yagamba nti tajja kwesimbawo ku lulwe kubanga mukakafu nti Museveni ajja kumuwa omulimu
Yagamba nti Museveni yamukubiriza okuva mu lwokaano alekere omummyuka wa ssentebe wa NRM mu Buggwanjuba bwa Uganda.
Matayo Kyaligonza yali mukakafu nti ajja kuweebwa omulimu mu kifo kyonna mu ggwanga.
Museveni ng'ekisinga okumubobbya omutwe mu kiseera kino kwe kugatta awamu abawagizi be oluvannyuma lw'okulonda kuno okw'okusunsulamu okutaagenda bulungi ate ng'ebulayo emyezi egitasukka mu ettaano okulonda kwa bonna kubeewo, alabika nga mumalirivu nnyo okukozesa enkola ye ey'okusuubiza abo abaagwa emirimu emirala mu kibiina kya NRM.
Aba NRM abamaze okunokolwayo tebalina kulowooza nti emirimu egy'okulondebwa abalonzi gye gyokka egiriwo.
Okusuubiza abantu emirimu kireeseewo obunkenke mu kampeyini za Museveni.
Dr Yasin Olum of Makerere University Political Science department says Uganda’s politics has become transactional, is no longer a service and Museveni will use it to maximum advantage	Dr. Yasin Olum ow'omu Yunivasite y'e Makerere mu kitongole ekisomesa eby'obufuzi agamba nti eby'obufuzi bwa Uganda bifuuse bya busuubuzi, kuno tekukyali kuweereza bantu era kino Museveni ajja kukikozesa nnyo kiganyula ye.
President Museveni will definitely achieve his immediate objective, which is keeping himself in power	Pulezidenti Museveni ajja kutuukiriza ekyo ky'ayagala, nga kino kwe kwenywereza mu buyinza.
”Olum, who is an expert on the democratisation process in Uganda, says the negative effects of the commercialisation of our politics will be borne by future generations	Olumu ate nga ye mukugu ku nsonga ezikwata ku demokulasiya mu Uganda, naye akabi akali mu kufuula eby'obufuzi okuba busineesi abanaabaawo mu biseera eby'omu maaso be bajja okwolekagana nabyo.
The Uganda constitution limits the number of ministers and their deputies to 42 but, in a bid to appease numerous political interests, Museveni has appointed 69 ministers and their deputies, hundreds of RDCs, Presidential Advisors, and other state agents	Ssemateeka wa Uganda akirambika nti baminisita mu Uganda awamu n'abammyuka baabwe balina kubeera 42, naye olw'okuba Museveni ayagala okubaako b'asanyusa mu by'obufuzi, alonze 69 awamu n'abammyuka baabwe, ne ba RDC bangi ddala, abawabuzi ba pulezidenti awamu n'abalala bangi.
For now, because it could jolt the gravy train ahead of the impending elections, Museveni cannot announce many new appointments but the job promises spewing out of State House suggest the legions of statesponsored leaches will increase in 2011	Museveni kino tayinza kukirangirira mu kiseera kino kubanga kiyinza okutabangula embeera naye eby'okusuubiza emirimu ebiva mu State House biraga nti omuwendo gwa baminisita gujja kulinnya nnyo mu 2011.
Critics say this places a huge burden on the national purse but Museveni maintains that it is the price of peace and proponents of the jobsforpeace in the NRM are equally adamant	Abeekenenya  bagamba nti kino kijja kuba muggugu gwa maanyi eri eby'enfuna by'eggwanga, naye ye Museveni agamba nti kino kyetaagisa okusobola okubaawo emirembe era ng'eno ye nkola ya NRM.
NRM Vice Chairman for Eastern Region, Mike Mukula says the strategy will work	Omummyuka wa ssentebe w'ekibiina kya NRM mu buvanjuba bwa Uganda Mike Mukula agamba nti enkola eno ejja kukola bulungi.
A party supporter who spoke out on condition of remaining anonymous says he was rigged out in the NRM elections in 2005 for MP in Mayuge district	Omuwagizi wa NRM atayagadde kwatuukirizibwa mannya agamba nti yabbibwa akalulu mu 2005 nga yeesimbyewo okulondebwa ng'omubaka wa palamenti mu disitulikiti y'e Mayuge.
He says Museveni and Hajji Moses Kigongo, at a meeting at the party headquarters on  Kyaddondo Road in Kampala, convinced him and others not to stand as independents on the understanding that they would work on the regional Museveni Task Force and later get jobs.	Agamba nti bwe baali ku lukuŋŋaana ku kitebbe ekikulu eky'ekibiina e Kyaddondo Road mu Kampala, Museveni ne Hajji Moses Kigongo baamumatiza nti ye n'abalala obuteesimbawo ku lwabwe kubanga baali bagenda kubeera mu abo abanaakulemberamu okunoonya akalulu n'oluvannyuma balifuna emirimu.
He says they held several meetings chaired by Sembabule District Chairperson Herman Sentongo as they toed with the idea of going independent	Agamba nti baabanga n'enkuŋŋaana nnyingi nga zikubirizibwa ssentebe wa disitulikiti y'e Sembabule Herman Sentongo era mu kiseera ekyo baali bamalirivu okwesimbawo ku bwabwe.
Rujumbura County MP and Chairman of NRM Veterans, Jim Muhwezi, says Museveni will deploy some of the losers within the party or the state and “facilitate others to carry out private business”	Omubaka wa palamenti ow'e Rujumbura era nga y'akola nga ssentebe w'abaazirwanako mu NRM, Jim Muhwezi, agamba nti Museveni ajja kuwa emirimu abamu ku abo abaawangulwa, mu kibiina mwenyini oba mu gavumenti, ate abalala abayambe okwekolera busineesi.
”Others, like Mutuluuza, are unlikely to pay attention to Muhwezi’s counsel	Abalala gamba nga Mutuluuza tebayinza kuwuliriza ebyo Muhwezi by'agamba.
Until his party, the NRM, endorsed Amelia, Mutuluuza’s seat was secure	Mutuluuza yali akkalidde mu kifo kye okutuusa ekibiina kye ekya NRM lwe kyaleeta Amelia.
The resident of Kammengo Township along KampalaMasaka highway remains very popular among his ethnic Banyarwanda who are a sizeable voting block in the constituency and has courted the other big voting blocks in his constituency, the Catholics and the Baganda establishment at Mengo	Omutuuze w'e Kammengo ekiri ku luguudo lw'e Masaka alina obuganzi bungi eri Banyarwanda banne abasinga obungi mu kitundu ekyo era ataddewo enkolagana n'abalonzi abalala era nga nabo bangi nnyo mu kitundu ekyo era bano be Bakatoliki n'abaganda abalina enkolagana ey'oku lusegere ne Mengo.
When in 2008-2009 Museveni’s government fought with the Mengo establishment over the acrimonious Land Amendment Bill 2007, Mutuluuza voted with Buganda and ganged up with Buganda legislators to force an emergency recall of parliament from recess to discuss the arrest of three Buganda Kingdom officials who had spoken out against the proposed land amendments	Mu 2008-2009 gavumenti ya Museveni bwe yalwanagana ne gavumenti y'e Mengo ku bikwata ku tteeka ly'ettaka erya 2007, Mutuluuza yali ku ludda lwa Buganda era ye ne bannabyabufuzi okuva mu Buganda bayita palamenti eyali egenze mu luwummula basobole okwogera ku ky'okukwata abakungu abasatu ab'omu Bwakabaka bwa Buganda abaali bavumiridde eky'okukola enoongosereza mu tteeka ly'ettaka.
Kyambadde tried to court ethnic Baganda by promising to engineer the return to air of the closed Buganda Kingdom radio station, CBS	Kyambadde yagezaako okusikiriza Abaganda ng'abasuubiza okuzaako laddiyo y'obwakabaka CBS eyali eggaliddwawo.
She used to move with some of the former workers of CBS, assuring supporters that she is working hard to switch the radio back on air and she is taking care of the interests of the former workers	Yatambulanga n'abamu ku abo abaali abakozi ba CBS ng'akakasa abawagizi be nti akola butaweera okuzzaako laddiyo era afaayo nnyo ku abo abaali abakozi ba laddiyo eyo.
Despite that, President Museveni appears to have anointed Amelia	Wadde nga kyali bwe kityo, kirabika ye Museveni yali yamala dda okulonda Amelia.
Sensing this, Mutuluuza opted to step outside the NRM, not participate in its primaries but run as an independent in 2011	Mutuluuza bwe yategeera ekyo, yasalawo okudda ebbali wa NRM, era teyeenyigira mu kammyufu k'ekibiina naye yeesimbawo ku lulwe mu 2011.
Museveni and Amelia know Mutuluuza could defeat them	Museveni ne Amelia bakimanyi nti Mutuluuza asobola okubawangula.
The Mawokota North MP is no stranger to battles with party big shots	Omubaka wa palamenti ow'e Mawokota atera okuba mu ntalo n'abanene abali mu kibiina.
He wrestled the constituency from an NRM strongman, the late former minister Zimula Mugwanya	Yalwanagana n'omunene omu mu kitundu ekyo, eyali minisita omugenzi Zimula Mugwanya.
In the heat of the acrimonious 2001 campaigns in which Mutuluuza accused Mugwanya of violently attacking his supporters, Mutuluuza is thought to have sponsored a court case in which Mugwanya was eventually thrown out of parliament for lack of academic qualifications	Mu kampeyini eyali enzibu ennyo eya 2001 Mutuluuza alyoke avunaane Mugwanya olw'okulumba abawagizi be mu ngeri ey'obukambwe, kigambibwa nti Mutuluuza yawangula omusango era Mugwanya n'aggyibwa mu palamenti olw'obutaba na buyigirize bumala.
Mugwanya was one of the financiers of the NRM bush war and his entourage on the campaign trail always had military escorts	Mugwanya yali omu ku abo abaawagira ennyo NRM mu by'ensimbi mu lutalo lw'omu nsiko era mu kampyeni ze kwabangako ab'amaggye.
Museveni’s hands tiedAs he weighs his next move, Museveni has been meeting with delegations from different areas where primary elections were chaotic and threatened his support	Emikono gya Museveni gisibiddwa emmabega era alowooza ku kiddako. Museveni abadde asisinkana abantu okuva mu bitundu eby'enjawulo okulonda gye kutagenda bulungi ne kiviirako abawagizi be okutya.
Museveni appears to merely seek opportunities to cajole, caution, and threaten	Kirabika nga Museveni ayagala okufuna akakisa okubalimba, okubakomako, n'okubatiisatiisa.
One such delegation came from Nakaseke district	Abamu ku bantu abo baava Nakaseke.
In Nakaseke, an NRM stronghold, antiriot police are still on patrol, and Finance Minister Syda Bbumba’s home is one of the highly guarded spots	Mu Nakaseke ate nga kye kimu ku bitundu NRM gy'erina obuwagizi obw'amaanyi, poliisi ekkakanya obujagalalo ekyalawuna, era n'amaka ga minisita w'eby'ensimbi Syda Bbumba ge gamu ku ago agasinze okukuumibwa.
The district was gripped in tension when one Nsamba Bukenya was declared winner of the NRM flagbearer contest for the district chair	Disitulikiti yalimu obunkenke bungi Nsamba Bukenya bwe yalangirirwa nga bwe yali omuwanguzi anaakwatira NRM bbendeera mu kifo kya ssentebe wa disitulikiti.
Incumbent chairperson, Ignatius Koomu, is believed to have won the election but the results were allegedly interchanged with those of Bukenya	Kigambibwa nti ssentebe aliko Koomu ye yawangula naye mbu ebyava mu kulonda byawanyisibwamu ne balangirira Bukenya
NRM delegates boo the party General Secretary Amama Mbabazi during the National Conference at Namboole on June 26	Abakiise mu ttabamiruka wa NRM eyali e Namboole mu Jjuuni nga 26 baalonda ssabawandiisi w'ekibiina kya NRM Amama Mbabazi.
Both Vice President Prof. Gilbert Bukenya and Trade Minister Maj. Gen. Kahinda Otafiire, who lost the secretary general post to Security Minister Mbabazi, have shown limited interest in party activities since the acrimonious showdown at Namboole	Bombi omummyuka wa pulezidenti Pro. Opponents accuse her of orchestrating a voterigging scheme that turned the results of the primary elections upside down	Abalabe be bamuvunaana nti yenyigira mu kubba obululu era kino ne kiviirako ebyali mu kulonda okwo obutaba bituufu.
The moment Bukenya was declared winner, spontaneous demonstrations broke out in the district	Kasita Bukenya yalangirirwa ku buwanguzi, waaliwo okwekalakasa mu disitulikiti.
Some 1,500 party cards were returned to the party offices in Semuto subcounty by angry supporters who felt their candidate had been robbed of victory	Kaada z'ekibiina eziwera nga 1500 zaakomezebwawo ku ofiisi y'ekibiina e Semuto ng'abawagizi bagamba nti oyo gwe babadde bawagira yabbibwa.
The demonstrators took to digging up the new tarmac road that is being built from Matugga to Butalangwa, the seat of the district administration	Abeekalakaasi baagenda ne batandika okusimmula ekkubo lya kolaasi eppya erizimbibwa okuva e Matugga okudda e Butalangwa awali ekitebe kya disitulikiti.
With the situation out of hand, Museveni invited a team from Nakaseke to explain to him what had happened	Olw'okuba embeera yali eyonoonese nnyo, Museveni alina be yayita okuva e Nakaseke bamubuulire ekyaliwo.
A source that attended the meeting says that Bbumba tilted the composition of the team to include many of her supporters who would misinform the president about the situation on the ground in Nakaseke	Abamu ku abo abaali mu lukuŋŋaana olwo bagamba nti Bumba yakyusa abo abaalina okugenda eri pulezidenti n'assaamu abawagizi be abandigambye Museveni ebitali bituufu ku mbeera eyali e Nakaseke.
“I felt uncomfortable throughout the meeting with the president because what was being fed to him was false but I was afraid to say the truth until Mubeezi, a resident of Ngoma subcounty, spoke out and informed the president that whatever he was being told was wrong,” the source told The Independent	Mu lukungaana olwo lwonna nnawulira nga siteredde olw'eby'obulimba ebyali bigambibwa pulezidenti naye nnali ntya okwogera amazima okutuusa Mubeezi, omu ku batuuze b'e ggombolola y'e Ngoma lwe yayogera n'agamba pulezidenti nti buli kye baali bamugamba si ge gaali amazima, waliwo ensonda ezaagamba The Independenti.
Ensonda zigamba nti, Mubeezi bwe yamala okwogera, yafuna abamuwagira okuva mu abo abaali bagenze okusisinkana pulezidenti era kino kyasobera nnyo pulezidenti.
Era ensonga zigattako nti, Museven alina be yasindika e Nakaseke okusobola okuzuula amazima gennyini ku ebyo ebyaliwo.
Abo be baatuma baakizuula nti abantu b'e Nakaseke baali baagala Koomu era nti okusinziira ku kino, ku ladiyo baalangirira nti Koomu gwe balonze okukwatira NRM bbendera mu disitulikiti y'e Nakaseke.

Karango nnamwandu w'omugenzi Private Edris Kyeyune eyafiira mu lutalo lw'okulwanyisa amaggye ga Kony, LRA
Karagaro agamba nti omulambo gwa bba gwakomezebwawo ne guziikibwa.
Karango agamba nti okuva mu 2004 abadde alina okuba ng'afuna ssente za bba eza pensoni okuva mu gavumenti naye wadde ng'afubye nnyo, tazifunanga.
Karango agamba nti ab'engaanda ze baali tebaagala alondoole ssente ezo era ne basalawo bakweke ebiwandiiko ebyali byetaagisibwa omuntu okusobola okufuna ssente ezo.
Karango ayambiddwako mukwano gwe ayitibwa Sirajj Musoke, naye nga mujaasi wa UPDF eyawummula olw'okuba nga mulwadde wa mukenenya era nga naye yeerwanyeeko nnyo okuva mu 2003 okusobola okufuna ssente ezo.
Musoke says that he has been helping several widows and orphans to secure their pension	Musoke agamba nti ayambye bannamwandu bangi ne bamulekwa okufuna ssente zaabwe
”Ann Kalenzi, 24, also says that she dropped out of school in S.3 when her father, Sgt Alex Kalenzi died in 2004 in a motor accident	Ann Kalenzi ow'emyaka 24 naye agamba nti okusoma yakukomya mu siniya yakusatu kitaawe Sgt Alex Kalenzi bwe yafiira mu kabanje ka mmotoka mu 2004.
Karango ne banne abalala abalina okufuna ssente za pensoni esuubi balirina mu abo bokka abaaliko abajaasi.
Kyokka, Felix Kulayigye omwogezi wa UPDF gyebuvuddeko awo yagamba nti Minisitule y'eby'Okwerinda emmaze okufuna ssente ez'okusasula abantu abo.
The audit titled “Pension Processing by the department of Compensation: ministry of Public Service” noted that “the general delays led to failure by retired officers to provide for themselves and their families leading to increased dependency burden, distress and frustration	Ekiwandiiko ekyaliko omutwe nti, Minisitule y'abakozi ekola ku kusasula ssente za pensoni" kyagamba nti okulwa okwo kuleetedde abajaasi abaawummula okulemererwa okwetuusaako era n'okutuusa ku b'omu maka gaabwe ebyetaago byabwe era kino ne kibaviirako okwesigama ku balala era n'okwenyamira.
Kulayigye agamba nti abajaasi abasukka mu 140,000 be baawandiisibwa era nga bano bajja kuganyulwa mu ssente obuwumbi 34 gavumenti ze yassaawo okusasula abajaasi bano.
Kulayigye era agamba nti waliwo n'obuwumbu obulala 120 obutegekeddwa ku lw'ekigendererwa kye kimu, kyokka zino era zijja kuweebwa n'abalala nga mw'otwalidde abaaliko aba poliisi n'abalala.
Era mu mbeera y'emu abo abaaliko abajaasi mu kiseera kya Amini ne Obote nabo mu butongole bajja kusiibulwa okuva mu maggye
Mu mwezi gwa Maaki 2009 kyagambibwa nti waliwo abaali babbye obuwumbi bwa ssente ezo ezaali aza abajaasi.
Emilio Mondo akulira Akakiiko akakola ku abo abaazirwanako era nga ye kennyini yenyigira mu kuwandiika abantu abo agamba nti, wadde nga tayinza kugamba nti abo abaali batalina kufuna ssente ezo baamalibwamu bonna, mukakafu nti bakendezebwa.
Mondo ate nga naye yaweereza mu maggye mu gavumenti ya Amini ne Obote, yalabirira okuwandisibwa kw'abantu abaukka mu mitwalo ataano mu West Nile ne mu mambuka ga Uganda.
Mondo agamba nti, tufuna okwemmulugunya okuva mu bantu baffe nti tebatuna ssente zaabwe, naye naffe tetumanyi bigenda mu maaso.
Naye mu lukungaana lwa UFA olwaliwo nga Sebutemba 22 ne 24 e Namboole, abaaluliko baagamba nti Kamya ayinza okuba ng'alemereddwa okuleetera abantu okukkiririza mu ndowooza z'ekibiina kye oba abo b'akozesa be bamuleetedde okulemererwa.
Ekibiina kya UFA ekikkiririza mu kutumbula enfuga ya federo kyalina ababaka baakyo mu divisoni ennya ez'omu Kampala, kwe kugamba, Rubaga, Makindye, Kawempe ne Nakawa era nga bino byali bitwalibwa nga disitulikiti.
Kanyeihamba nga ye mukwanaganya w'ekibiina kya UFA yagamba nti abo baali kitundu ky'abakiise 12,000 abaali basuubirwa mu lukungaana
E Mukono ne Wakiso tewavaayo bakiise; ebitundu bino birimu Abaganda ababadde baagala enfuga ya Federo okuviira ddala mu kiseera kya Sir Kabaka Edward Muteesa ow'olubereberye.
Mu Apuli 2010, katono ekibiina kisazibwemu kubanga kyawaayo bamemba abataaliwo okuva mu disitulikiti y'e Masindi, Buliisa, Kibaale, Iganga ne mu bifo ebirala mu ggwanga bwe kyayitibwa akakiiko k'eby'okulonda kiweeyo amannya g'ababaka amakumi attaano okuva mu disitulikiti za Uganda.

Nga Ssebutemba 20, Kanyeihamba yagamba nti abo be baalondera e Kawempe baali ba njawulo era baali bazingiramu abo abakiikirira abakazi, abavubuka n'abantu abaliko obulemu.

Kamya ye mukyala yekka ali mu lwokaano ku abo abeesimbyewo era ye mukyala ow'okubiri okuvuganya mu kifo ekya waggulu mu ggwanga, eyasooka yali Miria Obote eyeesimbawo mu 2006 okuvuganya ku bwa pulezidenti ng'asinziira mu kibiina kya UPC.

Mu munisipaali y'e Rukungiri, akulira abakya mu FDC Ingrid Turinawe, yawangulwa Roland Mugume, ssentebe wa disitulikiti.
Bwe yakkiriza okuwangulibwa Turinawe yagamba nti okulonda kwali kwa mazima na bwenkanya naye n'agamba nti ajja kwesimbawo avuganye ku kifo ky'omubaka omukyala owa disitulikiti avuganye minisita Sezi Mbaguta.
